Foreign Important Telegrams

Seven National Statesmen Meet and Negotiate Restoration of German Finance

Short-term credit loan to Germany

France's unique objection

British authorities prepare to visit Germany

Large amounts of cash sent from England to France

▲Reuters, London, 22nd: Reuters learned last night that there was no unanimous agreement on the plan to restore German credit. The London Conference now seems to be proceeding in dim light of conflicting opinions. The current situation is extremely difficult, and it is expected that the fate of the London Conference will be decided at the plenary session on Wednesday. The conference will listen to some of the proposals made at the finance official meeting and try to assimilate them. Attendees of the finance official meeting are keeping everything very secret. This alone has triggered alarming rumors, and the responsible parties have issued denials that the opinions of the representatives differ. It is worth noting that President Hoover's new plan has not yet been considered. London legal persons expect the conference to end on Thursday. British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Secretary Henderson will send a copy to the German Prime Minister and others to return to Germany this week.

▲Reuters, London, 21st: This morning's Seven Nations Conference lasted two and a half hours. Attendees all acknowledged that the most important part of today's difficulties is to discuss the method of international financial cooperation in order to quickly restore the solid credit of the German economy. It was agreed that the first step must be to stop asking Germany for loans. U.S. Secretary of State Stimson is confident that U.S. banks can continue to cooperate to maintain German credit and hopes that banks in other countries will also adopt the same plan and attitude. The finance officials met for five and a half hours in the afternoon and issued a press release at the end of the meeting. The wording was very brief, only saying that the results obtained will be submitted to the plenary session to be held tomorrow morning. It was heard that the most discussed issue was how to enable Germany to overcome its current difficulties.

▲National, London, 21st: Today, London is widely rumored that France has refused to participate in the plan to provide short-term loans to German banks without requiring guarantees, but Japan seems to be able to join. The French representatives have prompted them to pay attention to this situation.

▲Reuters, Washington, 21st: The U.S. proposal to rescue Germany discussed the German economic panic, saying that the key point of this matter is to restore German economic life, and also discussed the political aspects of this panic, saying that the U.S. government hopes that European countries will reduce conflicts, so that the world can rely on the safety of European politics. As for Germany's current predicament, it can be said to be a panic of short-term loans. The foundation on which these short-term debts are based is sound and certain, but the general uncertainty in recent weeks has caused a major shock to the German financial structure. There are two forms of shock: one is the outflow of marks from Germany, and the other is the withdrawal of foreign deposits and the reduction of debts by foreign banks. Fundamentally, there is no reason for this action. The current predicament can be resolved immediately and effectively through cooperative behavior. Secretary of State Stimson submitted the new U.S. proposal to the London Conference, which was sent by President Hoover to Stimson and Yimu on Friday and has now been announced by Acting Secretary of State Kessel. What it advocates is that bankers from various countries should have an agreement to maintain the short-term debts that have already been lent to Germany, totaling $1,200,000,000. An international committee should be established as an international cooperation agency to maintain this debt, and it should immediately consider converting a part of this short-term debt into long-term debt. This international committee can be placed under the Bank for International Settlements.

▲Reuters, New York, 21st: The U.S. government's proposal to rescue Germany is in line with the opinions of important U.S. bankers.

Some bankers believe that Germany can overcome this crisis with its government's and national bank's strong plan. After domestic and foreign credit is restored, a part of Germany's short-term debt can be converted into long-term debt.

▲Reuters, Washington, 21st: Responsible parties claim that although Secretary of State Stimson discussed the general idea of the U.S. plan to rescue Germany with officials from various countries in London yesterday, other suggestions regarding the German rescue can be considered. However, the U.S. plan is a requirement that has been considered and carefully deliberated and cannot be changed much. From this, it can be seen that the U.S. attitude towards the London Conference has been decided.

▲National, Berlin, 21st: According to news from England, regarding the rescue of German finances, the issue of political guarantees has been clearly shelved at the London Seven Nations Conference. The issue of financial guarantees has not been raised. The large loan of 200 million marks, which was previously proposed to be secured by German tariffs and repaid in ten years, has also been abandoned. The countries at the conference believe that Germany's current difficulties can be resolved with short-term loans and that there is no need to study issues such as political guarantees.

▲Reuters, London, 21st: After the adjournment of the plenary session of the London Conference, the Finance Officials Committee met with the British and German Prime Ministers and the Belgian representative in the Prime Minister's office in the House of Commons. It started at 3:30 pm and lasted until 9:00 pm, with only one short break. The results of the discussion will be submitted to the plenary session at 10:00 am tomorrow.

▲Reuters, New York, 22nd: Wall Street is now gradually believing that the German financial panic will eventually lead to the resurgence of the entire issue of war debts and reparations. It is expected that at least the payment will be reduced. The New York Tribune reported that President Hoover's proposal to maintain Germany's existing debt has not aroused any responsiveness from New York bankers. New York bankers believe that helping Germany from the outside lies in reducing or eliminating the payment of reparations. What bankers are worried about is that even if debt to Germany continues, people will rush to withdraw cash when the debt matures, and another panic will inevitably occur.

▲Dentsu, London, 21st: The Bank of England announced today that it has sold gold bars worth £2,829,499 and shipped them to France. In the past eight days, gold bars worth £12 million have been shipped from England to France. The financial community is paying close attention to this. France is now working hard to accumulate gold, and its gold reserves are greater than those of the United States.

France's Attitude Towards Disarmament

Replying to the League of Nations in Six Items

Guaranteeing Security as a Prerequisite

▲National, Paris, 21st: France's response to the League of Nations' inquiry about the current state of armaments and its attitude towards disarmament consists of 28 pages. Its main points are: (1) Disarmament must be based on security; (2) If a country is invaded, France is willing to cooperate with it without reservations, regardless of the form, according to formal combat based on mutual assistance; (3) The maximum level of armaments stipulated in the treaty does not necessarily require other countries to regard it as a standard; (4) The general issue of limiting armaments contains more political nature than technical nature, so it cannot be solved with anemometric tables and arbitrary reduction percentages; (5) The reduction of armaments can be proportional to the degree of mutual assistance among countries resisting aggression; (6) Please pay attention to France's position. In the past century, France has experienced three foreign invasions.

Hurricane Passes Through Poland

Trees Uprooted, Houses Collapsed, Traffic Blocked

Thirty People Killed, More Than Three Hundred Injured

▲National, Warsaw, 21st: An unprecedented hurricane occurred in the Juping area of Poland, causing a rare and huge disaster. Internal and external traffic was completely cut off, and the report only reached the capital this morning. The army and medical teams were able to go to rescue. According to those who witnessed the disaster, the hurricane was truly a rare disaster. Thousands of large trees were uprooted, the roofs of many houses were blown off, and trains were blown off the rails. A car with three people in it was blown ten meters into the air before falling, killing four people. According to the latest investigation, thirty people were killed and more than three hundred were injured in this disaster. There have been no reports from the affected areas in neighboring districts, and the losses may be much greater.

Russian Army Minister Arrives in Boli

▲Reuters, Moscow, 21st: Today, it was announced here that Soviet Russian Army Minister Voroshilov has arrived in Boli, a city near the Russian-Manchurian border, to meet with General Belutsky, Commander of the Special Far East Army.

Confirmed by the Wilson Observatory

▲Dentsu, Cambridge (Massachusetts, USA), 21st: The Harvard University Observatory announced today that the Wilson Observatory's (California) research results have confirmed the existence of the Nagata Comet recently discovered by the Japanese. It is not yet clear whether the Nagata Comet is a star in the solar system.

Special Article

A Study on the Immigration of Koreans to the Northeast (Bin)

(I) Introduction

Since the Wanbaoshan Incident occurred, I have written articles discussing the matter, advising the Japanese, and encouraging my fellow countrymen. However, as of today, the number of Koreans who have immigrated to the Northeast has exceeded one million. This has become an extremely serious problem in our country's politics and economy. Although the National Internal Affairs Conference discussed this issue this year, many of the resolutions have not been put into practice. Koreans still live in mixed communities as before, and free immigration continues as before. Furthermore, disputes are on the rise, driven by a purposeful conspiracy and supported by a portion of the Korean people as its pawns. Thus, over the years, all parts of our Northeast have been rife with disputes. Infringements of sovereignty and all kinds of unreasonable bullying often occur under a planned and methodical course of action, causing significant harm to our country. Our government knows that this problem is extremely important, but it shies away from addressing it, and has taken no appropriate countermeasures or positive actions for a long time. It has been unable to restrict the entry of Koreans, nor has it been able to supervise their activities, allowing the advance troops of conspirators to come in droves, penetrating our heartland. The occurrence of the Wanbaoshan Incident was no accident. The future is long, and if this problem is not properly resolved, it is not difficult for us to foresee what serious situations will occur in the years to come. After the Wanbaoshan Incident, the Japanese government expressed its intention to negotiate a solution to the immigration problem with us. Its intention was nothing more than to use its cunning diplomatic tactics to obtain a formal basis for immigrating Koreans to our Northeast. The seriousness and urgency of the situation mean that our country can no longer delay and postpone action. Thorough preparation, planning, and appropriate countermeasures are now crucial. Otherwise, future hidden dangers will be unimaginable. Looking to the future, I am deeply concerned. Therefore, despite my limited knowledge, I will present the facts and express my views to alert my countrymen, and deeply hope that my countrymen will rise up together to discuss it.

(II) Japan's Policy of Immigrating Koreans

When the Russo-Japanese War ended, Japanese Foreign Minister Komura Jutarō had a plan to immigrate four million people to "Mongolia and Manchuria" within twenty years. Later, during the Terauchi Cabinet, Foreign Minister Gotō Shinpei also boasted of immigrating 500,000 people to Manchuria and Mongolia within ten years. However, due to (1) the climate and living conditions of our Northeast are not suitable for Japanese people to live in; (2) the living standards of farmers in Japan are higher than those of farmers in our Northeast; (3) Japanese farmers are not as hardworking and resilient as farmers in our Northeast; and (4) the rapid influx of immigrants from inland China to the Northeast. Because of these four points, Japanese farmers are far from being able to compete with Northeast farmers. Therefore, although Japanese political and economic forces have directly extended into our Northeast for decades, and they have been plotting to immigrate to our Northeast, to this day, the number of Japanese people in the Northeast is only over 200,000. Among them, employees of the South Manchuria Railway and other institutions and companies account for the absolute majority. Only three or four thousand people are actually engaged in farming and fishing. Japan's policy of immigrating its people to "Mongolia and Manchuria" has failed in practice, but it will never give up its original plan because of this. As a result, the "indirect immigration policy" has arisen instead. The so-called indirect immigration is to have Japanese people move to Korea, and then force Koreans to enter our Northeast. This is because the living standards of Koreans are similar to those of the Chinese, and their spirit of hard work and resilience in managing farming is also similar. Therefore, Koreans are used as the vanguard for invading our Northeast, while the Japanese monopolize Korea and reap the benefits. At the same time, although the Japanese rulers in Korea have exhausted their ability to suppress the people, the Eight Provinces of Korea still occasionally show signs of instability. The calls for national restoration are repeated again and again. The implementation of the indirect immigration policy will disperse the unity of the Korean people, and the movement for national restoration will become even more difficult. It will be easier to rule the Korean people. This is an important background to the immigration of Koreans to the Northeast. The "Policy for Promoting and Protecting Korean Immigration" in the Tanaka Cabinet's memorandum on the "Positive Policy Towards Manchuria and Mongolia" further illuminates the ruthlessness of its conspiracy. An excerpt is as follows:

"Since Korea merged with us, it may be temporarily prosperous. However, after the European War, the American President advocated national self-determination, like an inspiration from heaven, to incite weak nations. The hearts of the Korean people were also incited, and an unstable atmosphere filled the Eight Provinces of Korea... Fortunately, Manchuria and Mongolia are full of abundant resources to settle Korean immigrants. As a result, the number of Korean immigrants is increasing day by day. Today, there are nearly one million Koreans in the three eastern provinces. This phenomenon allows the Empire to obtain rights and interests in Manchuria and Mongolia without seeking them. It can truly be said that the country has created great happiness, and it adds countless forces to the Empire's national defense and economy in Manchuria and Mongolia. It reveals a great dawn for the rule of the Korean people. The masses of Koreans immigrating to the three eastern provinces can open up the virgin lands of Manchuria and Mongolia for the motherland, so that the motherland can make progress. Furthermore, Koreans can be used as a stepping stone to connect with the Chinese people in every aspect. On one hand, we can utilize Koreans who have naturalized as Chinese citizens to massively buy up rice paddies and land in Manchuria and Mongolia. On the other hand, we can use credit cooperatives or banks in various places to provide funds to those Koreans with Chinese citizenship to serve as command towers for our economic invasion. We can also increase food production to save the country from danger. This is also an opportunity to develop new colonies. The naturalized Koreans are nominally naturalized citizens of China, but they will eventually return to our nationality...

They only naturalize as Chinese citizens for temporary convenience. According to our plan, if the number of Koreans in Manchuria and Mongolia expands to more than 2.5 million, we can use the Koreans as a nuclear force for military activities when the time comes. Furthermore, we can aid their actions under the pretext of suppression. In addition, among the Koreans in Manchuria and Mongolia, some have naturalized as Chinese citizens, and some have not. When the time comes, we can use the tactic of 'selling dog meat under the pretense of selling sheep heads' to deal with whether it is the Chinese Koreans who are causing trouble or the Japanese Koreans. However, although our country can utilize Koreans to act in this way, we must also be prepared for the Chinese government to use Koreans to control us...

In addition, if our country wants to develop new continents, the protection and suppression of Korea must be even more serious. Therefore, based on the Three Arrows Treaty, we are allowed to establish police stations all over northern Manchuria, and we must greatly expand and fill them with police force in order to appease the Korean people and aid their rapid advancement... Although we have abandoned the special rights of the Ishii-Lansing Agreement, we can use the new problem of Korean immigration to restore our special rights in Manchuria and Mongolia. Under such circumstances, when we restore our special rights, no one in the international community will dare to oppose our actions under the law."

Furthermore, Fujiwara Kei also discussed this issue in his book "Eastern Provinces Must Be Taken Seriously." He said:

"...Japan's immigration to Manchuria and Mongolia, after more than twenty years, is only 180,000. It can be determined to be hopeless. The only national policy is to send Koreans, who can compete with the Chinese in economic warfare and have special skills in developing rice paddies, to Manchuria and Mongolia to indirectly guide the development of Manchuria and Mongolia and solve Japan's population and food problems. There is no other strategy for the Japanese to develop the mainland. To put it bluntly, Koreans are just a signboard. Therefore, the solution to this problem is related to the survival of Japan. If it cannot reach the highest level, the development of Manchuria and Mongolia will be dull, and the world will doubt the strength of ruling Korea. The solution to this problem is so important and delicate, and the solution must be rapid and fundamental. But what is the fundamental solution?"

"In solving this problem, the Japanese government must resolutely resolve the long-standing issue of commercial lease rights, guarantee the freedom of commercial lease, residence, and business... "

By examining the Tanaka Memorandum and the arguments of Tenggang Kei, we can see that Japan's immigration of Koreans to the Northeast is clearly not just a simple matter of immigration for food. Its conspiracy and ambition lie in promoting its mainland policy. And the ruthlessness of its methods and the subtlety of its implementation make us shudder. For decades, our borderlands have been under its covert attacks, blithely unaware, eventually creating hidden dangers in our heartland. Looking back on the past, how can we not feel sorrow? This is what our government should learn from today. (To be continued)

According to reports from Ping, since the apostasy of Shi Yousan, telegrams between Ping and Han encountered obstacles yesterday afternoon (the 18th) and could not be directly transmitted. Eight Northeast aircraft teams arrived in Ping this morning (the 18th). More will be transferred into the Pass as needed. After the attitude of the Central Army in Henan, which had detained vehicles by Shi, changed, its plainclothes reconnaissance team secretly attacked Neiqiu. After our army fought back, they retreated to Baixiang. Shi, aware of the difficult environment, is isolated and his plan seems to have changed. Chairman Wang (Shuchang) has gone to inspect the Jinpu Road and will return to Tianjin within a few days and then come to Ping. Pingjin may implement martial law temporarily if necessary." The Second Team of Northeast Armored Trains arrived in Ping from Shenyang a few days ago. At 11:30 last night, the 18th, Zhou Yongye led them from the West Station to Baoding. He himself led the armored train to Baoding to await orders. The First Team is currently stationed in Xinle.

The General Affairs Office of the Deputy Commander-in-Chief's Headquarters sent a letter to the newspapers yesterday, stating, "To All Newspapers: At this time of military brewing, various newspapers are picking up unfounded rumors as news material, which is most likely to cause alarm and affect public safety. In today's newspapers, it is reported that Shi Yousan is acting freely, and that Chairman Han of Shandong and the generals of Shanxi are also unanimously supporting him. It has been found that Shi Yousan's act of betraying the country and inciting rebellion has already been revealed. If it is unavoidable to use force, this headquarters, together with the Central Army, will declare his crimes and punish him. It will not be long before he can be suppressed. Chairman Han of Shandong and the generals of Shanxi are aware of the righteousness and have been sending telegrams in recent days requesting joint efforts to punish him. There will be no change. The reports in the newspapers are close to instigating behavior, which is most taboo in military times. Therefore, this letter is to inform you that in the future, the newspapers should not publish any military news about Shandong, Shanxi, and nearby provinces, so as to avoid confusion. Your newspaper has a sympathetic understanding of maintaining the local area and will support this intention. If anyone disregards the overall situation and publishes intentionally provocative articles, this headquarters will resolve it according to law in order to maintain order and facilitate military operations, and to serve as a warning to others. This letter is hereby sent and should be noted. General Affairs Office of the Deputy Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force."

According to reports from Tianjin, the defense of the Jinpu Road is the responsibility of Wang Shuchang, Commander of the Second Army. Wang, accompanied by his Chief of Staff Chen Qinruo and the two brigade commanders Chang Jiwu and Yao Dongfan, inspected the defense of the Cangzhou area the day before yesterday. He returned to Tianjin by special train at about 1:00 a.m. yesterday (the 18th). He went to the provincial government to work at noon. At 6:00 p.m., he hosted a banquet for Ban Chan. At 8:00 p.m., he gathered soldiers from the Twenty-First Regiment at Cai's Garden for instructions. Brigade Commander Yao Dongfan also accompanied him to the scene. After Wang gave instructions, he gave separate instructions to the officers until about 9:00 p.m. Other troops stationed in Tianjin will also be given instructions in turn. (19th)

Shandong in the Serious Situation in the North

▲ Han Fuqu Dispatches Troops to Guard Against Shi's Troops

Jinan Correspondence, the north and south of Shandong, Guan Valley, is particularly important in this serious situation in the north. Provincial Chairman Han Fuqu has expressed his support for peace and obedience to the Commander-in-Chief and Deputy Commander-in-Chief. Therefore, all divisions of his troops are stationed in their original defenses and have not been transferred. However, yesterday he specially sent Zhang Yue of the Provincial Committee, along with Jiang Bocheng and Fan Pujiang, representatives of Deputy Commander Zhang, to Ping to meet with Deputy Commander Zhang to request instructions on everything. Yesterday morning, he received a telegram from Jiang and Zhang, stating that the trip was very successful. Therefore, the troops of this province began to move towards the border between Hebei and Shandong to cooperate with the Northeast Army in providing appropriate defense against Shi's troops. As for the Zhao Xuande Brigade of Sun Tongxuan's division, which was originally stationed in Dexian County, it has now been decided to send Cao Fulin again to sit in Dexian. Other troops in western Shandong, such as the entire Rong Guangxing Brigade originally stationed in Dongchang, and the entire Li Hanzhang Brigade originally stationed in Jining, have very solid defenses. Yesterday morning, Han personally went to Xinzhuang and gathered the officers and soldiers of Cao's division and Li's brigade to give instructions, urging them to protect the local area, care for the people, and diligently train after arriving in various counties.

Li Shuchun, Director of the Civil Affairs Department, told reporters yesterday that the situation in the north still has hope of turning around. Even if it unfortunately breaks down, Shandong will not fall into the vortex. However, the counties in northern and western Shandong border Hebei and Henan. When the situation is not peaceful, it is inevitable that bandits will take the opportunity to harass, and dismissed soldiers will recklessly think of summoning troops, thereby disturbing local security. Therefore, I have carefully selected the county magistrates and public security bureau chiefs of the counties in the northwest and replaced them entirely with those who have military knowledge, so that they can suppress bandits at any time and easily connect with the military, so as to achieve the effect of commanding as one's own arms.

According to a report from a certain party, Xue Chuanfeng, a bandit army that has been disturbing western Shandong for a long time, recently returned south from Pingjin, got on the train in Dezhou, and was accompanied by four other people. At that time, the military police were deceived and went away freely. When the military police discovered it, they reported to the province on the one hand and sent people to track them on the other hand, but they finally escaped. It is reported that Bandit Xue is now in Fan County and there are rumors of occupying two villages. It is also reported that Bandit Xue was commissioned by Shi Yousan to plan to recruit bandits in western Shandong. The provincial government has now telegraphed Rong Guangxing's troops stationed in Dongchang to go nearby to strictly suppress them.

Capital Circles Anti-Japanese Protection of Overseas Chinese General Assembly

▲ Sending Representatives to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to Lodge a Serious Protest

▲ Resolving to Request the Central Government to Designate the 7/3 National Humiliation Day

▲ Shouting Slogans Such as Economic Severance with Japan

The series of events in the capital, including the occurrence of the Korean violence against Chinese in various Shu areas, the Japanese imperialists' failure to prevent it beforehand, and their lack of protection during the incident, reveal their conspiracy to exploit the situation and provoke our country to fulfill their ambition of sending troops to Manchuria. This is obvious. It is believed that nothing could be more contemptuous of our nation, in violation of humanitarianism and international law, than this. If we do not swiftly plan countermeasures, how can we maintain our own survival? Therefore, various organizations have gathered to form the Anti-Japanese Protection of Overseas Chinese and National Salvation Assembly, which will convene at the Yang Gong and National Grand Theater at 8:00 AM on the 22nd. Xiao Jishan, the executive member of the Municipal Party Department, was elected as chairman. After feeling grief, people from all walks of life who attended the meeting were unanimously inspired to rise up. The details of the meeting are recorded as follows:

▲ A Glimpse of the Venue At the entrance of the venue, there were registration desks for representatives from various circles, with the Municipal Party Department Boy Scouts maintaining order. Anti-Japanese slogans were hung everywhere inside and outside the venue. The Propaganda Department of the Municipal Party Department, the Overseas Chinese Associations in Beijing, the Overseas Chinese in Siam, the Asian Cultural Association, and the Federation of Eastern Oppressed Nationalities distributed leaflets denouncing Japanese imperialism in the venue to awaken the general public.

▲ Meeting Order (1) Opening of the meeting, (2) Playing music, (3) Singing the Party song, (4) Bowing three times to the Party and National flags and the portrait of the Premier, (5) The Chairman respectfully reading the will, (6) The entire audience observing three minutes of silence for the overseas Chinese compatriots who died in Korea, (7) The Chairman delivering the opening address, (8) Representatives giving speeches, (9) Shouting slogans, (10) Playing music, (11) Adjournment of the meeting.

▲ Enthusiastic Participation The presidium attending the meeting included Xiao Jishan from the Municipal Party Department, Ma Jun from the business community, Lin Qinglong from the agricultural community, Zhu Shanglin from the academic community, Jia Guomin from the labor community, Zhang Shuzhen from the women's community, Luo Zeqi from the overseas Chinese community, and Shi Weihuan and Lai Lian, executive members of the Municipal Party Department. Approximately 2,000 to 3,000 representatives from military and political agencies and various people's organizations attended.

▲ Chairman's Address Chairman Xiao Jishan delivered an address, stating that the compatriots and comrades attending the meeting today should have four understandings of the Wanbaoshan Incident and the Korean violence against Chinese: (1) It is entirely backed by Japanese imperialists, using Koreans as the vanguard to infringe upon China; (2) The Japanese imperialists are treating the overseas Chinese in Korea as weak nations, oppressing and trampling on them by any means. Our party must uphold the principle of supporting the world's weak nations, unite with the world's weak nations, rise up to defend the nation and the world, and overthrow the imperialists' ambition to oppress humanity; (3) The Japanese invasion policy is to move Koreans to Manchuria and Mongols and move their own people to Korea. Therefore, compatriots across the country should concentrate their efforts to enrich and develop the Northeast to prevent their covetousness; (4) The Japanese imperialists' persecution of our compatriots is no different from the atrocities of the Red imperialists. All our people should use the determination and strength to eliminate the Red bandits and overthrow Japanese imperialism.

▲ Representatives' Speeches Luo Zeqi, the representative of the overseas Chinese in Beijing, Wu Mai, the representative of the National Lawyers Association, Ma Jun, the representative of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Jia Guomin, the representative of the labor community, Zhu Shanglin, the representative of the academic community, Jiang Mengchi, the representative of the Chinese workers in France, and others spoke successively. Their main points were: (1) The whole country should unite as the government's diplomatic backing, and strive to achieve the goals of punishing the perpetrators, providing compensation, offering condolences, apologizing, and ensuring that no more atrocities occur in the future; (2) How long has it been since the Jinan Massacre, and yet this tragic incident has occurred again? We have to blame the weakness and incomplete resolution of previous diplomacy and the failure of the general public to be firm and persistent in economic severance and boycotting inferior goods. In the future, we must have an organized and determined approach to severance and boycotting goods, adopting extremely effective methods and adhering to the end, without taking advantage of the opportunity to seek personal gain, so as not to be despised by foreigners and mocked again for "five minutes of enthusiasm." It is hoped that the government will no longer collect taxes on imported Japanese goods to avoid excuses. Anyone who purchases Japanese goods should be reported by the merchant and severely punished.

▲ Representatives' Petition After the representatives finished their speeches, most of the representatives proposed that Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting attend to explain the diplomatic policy for this tragic incident and the current state of progress. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs was notified by telephone and replied that Minister Wang was attending the Central Political Conference and was not in the ministry. Therefore, someone in the meeting proposed to go to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to question as a whole. After discussion by the presidium, in order to be cautious, there was no need for a mass parade. Twenty-eight representatives were elected as petition representatives to go to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to petition for serious negotiations on this case until a satisfactory result was achieved.

▲ General Assembly Proposals The proposals passed by the General Assembly that day: (1) Establish the Capital Circles Anti-Japanese Protection of Overseas Chinese and National Salvation Association as soon as possible, organized by business, academic, agricultural, labor, women's, and other groups; (2) Implement permanent economic severance with Japan from today, which will be handled by the Capital Circles Anti-Japanese Protection of Overseas Chinese and National Salvation Association; (3) Raise funds to comfort the overseas Chinese who died in the disaster; (4) Submit a request to the Central Government to instruct the National Government to find ways to provide funds for the overseas Chinese who have left Korea to return to Korea to continue working; (5) Request the National Government to order the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to implement revolutionary diplomacy until the goals of compensation, apology, and guarantee are achieved; (6) Request the National Government to automatically abolish all unequal treaties and special privileges between China and Japan; (7) Request the National Government to strictly crack down on the case of Koreans with dual nationality; (8) Tell the Korean compatriots oppressed by Japan to make them realize; (9) Announce the truth of the tragic incident to the whole world to expose Japan's cruel actions; (10) Hold regular memorial services for the overseas Chinese who died in the disaster; (11) Organize a large-scale propaganda team to publicize the truth about the Wanbaoshan and Korean cases; (12) Request the National Government to order the Ministries of Foreign Affairs and Transportation to recover the right to navigate inland rivers and prohibit Chinese people from taking Japanese ships; (13) Request the National Government to dismiss and punish Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting for flattering foreigners and seeking glory, harming rights, and humiliating the country; (14) Request the National Government to eliminate internal strife and unite against foreign enemies; (15) Submit a request to the Central Government to establish an International Propaganda Bureau; (16) Submit a request to the Central Government to actively prepare for military equipment as a diplomatic backing; (17) Request the Central Government to designate July 3 as the National Humiliation Memorial Day for the Japanese massacre of overseas Chinese; (18) Request the government to issue a decree to punish Shi Yousan, who plotted rebellion, as soon as possible; (19) Submit a request to the Central Government to instruct all party members to implement military training in order to declare war on Japan; (20) Request the National Government to instruct the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to dismiss and punish the Korean Consul.

Ningdu, the Base of Unshorn Hair, Completely Recovered

▲ The Suppression Army Fought Fiercely with the Bandits for Three Days and Nights

▲ The Remnant Bandits Fled to Donggu, Xingguo, and Ruijin

Nanchang Correspondence, Ningdu is located in southern Jiangxi and is biased to the east. To the east, it can go to Guangchang and Shicheng to connect to western Fujian. To the south, it can pass through Huichang and Ruijin to enter Guangdong. To the west, it can cross the Gan River from Yudu and Xingguo to enter Hunan. To the north, it is bordered by Le'an, Nanfeng, and Yihuang in eastern Jiangxi. To the northwest, it is intertwined with Yongfeng. The Dashanling and Xueheling mountains meander between them. The mountains and forests are lush, with the Meijiang River flowing southwest into the Gan River. There are many plains on both sides, the land is fertile, and the people are simple. Ningcheng is located on the right of the Meijiang River and is quite prosperous. Since Zhu Mao fled from the west bank of the Gan River to the east of the Gan River and the southern part of Jiangxi last year, he has used this as a base. The pseudo-revolutionary committee, the pseudo-central Soviet, and the pseudo-military committee were mostly set up here. Important bandit leaders such as Zhu Mao, Peng Huang, etc. lurked in it, issuing orders, not only burning, killing, and looting all of Jiangxi, but also being the major camp of the Red bandits in the five southeastern provinces. Its importance can be imagined. Since Zhu Bandit occupied Ningdu last year, the nearby counties of Guangchang, Shicheng, Ruijin, Huichang, Yudu, Xingguo, Ji'an, Yongfeng, and Le'an have been invaded and occupied by the Red bandits one after another. Bandits were dispatched to set up pseudo-workers' and peasants' associations and pseudo-Soviet governments everywhere, using hooligans and ruffians to create red terror. The middle and upper classes had no other way than death or escape. Those who stayed in the local area were forced to join the bandits. The central government paid great attention to this. This time, Commander-in-Chief Chiang came to Jiangxi to supervise the suppression, with Ningdu as the biggest target, and the advance of the central, left, and right routes was also to meet in Ningdu as the most important task. When the left wing successively recovered Lichuan, Kangdu, Guangchang, Jianning, and Shicheng, the main force of the Red bandits fled to Ningdu. The suppression army also tailed and attacked Ningcheng, and a part was stationed in Tangtang and Gaotian in the area bordering Guangchang, Shicheng, and Jianning Ninghua to block the Fujian bandits from attacking and consolidate the rear. On the 15th of this month, the suppression army occupied Toupi and Hengtian to the east of Ningdu, only tens of miles away from Ningcheng. At that time, the pseudo-Third Army Huang Gonglue, the pseudo-Fourth Army Lin Biao, and the pseudo-Twelfth Army Chen Yi and other troops in Ningcheng attacked in full force, guarding the highlands in the Wutoushan Xianqiaoshan area. The suppression army fiercely fired at the bandit's position, with bullets raining down, but because of the uphill attack, it was not easy to succeed. From the 17th to the 19th, the suppression army used machine guns, artillery, and aircraft to cover the bandits in hand-to-hand combat, charging back and forth, killing countless bandits. The bandits, seeing that the situation was not good, collapsed and retreated one after another. The suppression army took advantage of the victory to pursue again, and the bandits abandoned the city and fled. The suppression army then completely recovered Ningbu. The remnant bandits collapsed and retreated in two parts. The bandits in northern Ning retreated into Gulonggang in Xingguo and southern Yongfeng to rescue Donggu. The bandits in southern Ning retreated to Ruijin and Huichang, echoing the bandits in Tinghang in western Fujian. However, the bandits were embarrassed, and the bridges along the way were destroyed to prevent the suppression army from pursuing. There were also many abandoned sick and wounded Red bandits. According to the news from the forward headquarters, the suppression army advanced lightly and quickly, and the bandits had nowhere to go. The fundamental elimination of the Red bandits will not be far away. Also, the Xingying received a victory telegram from Zhu Shaoliang yesterday, roughly stating that after our army deleted the front and rear of Toupiyi occupied on the day, the bandits Huang Gonglue and Chen Yi came to resist from Ningdu in full force. In the Wutoushan Xianqiaoshan area, there was a fierce battle for three days and nights. After our armies fought bravely and fiercely, and engaged in hand-to-hand combat, the bandit's entire line was broken and tracked and pursued. Our armies successively occupied Ningdu City on Haori. The remaining bandits fled to the old nest of Donggu. In this battle, countless rice and weapons were captured, and about 30,000 coerced people were dissolved, and thousands of ransom tickets were released, etc. (July 21)

Ruan's Division Broke Through Fang Bandit's Old Nest

▲ Red Bandits in Eastern Jiangxi Lost Another Base

Nanchang Correspondence, Fang Zhimin's bandit nest in eastern Jiangxi was broken by Ruan's division last night, the 16th. According to news from the Xingying, Zhang's brigade of Ruan's division set out from Lingxi Bridge at dawn on the 16th to search and advance to Ge Yuan, the border between Shangrao and Hengfeng. First, the bandits guarding Fengxiangling were defeated, and they arrived at Ge Yuan that evening. They defeated more than 2,000 Red bandits and occupied Fang Bandit's old nest and destroyed various pseudo-agencies. Ge Yuan is located north of Hengfeng and is the base of Fang Bandit. The victory telegram of Ruan Zhaochang is recorded below to see the battle situation on that day. The telegram said, "Zhang Xian, the brigade commander of the Division of the Profession, telegraphed Shen, the brigade set out from Lingxi at 3:00 AM to search and suppress Ge Yuan. The vanguard Li Regiment passed through Fengxiangling and encountered more than 700 bandits with 400 to 500 guns in the evening, occupying the hilltop to resist. After the Mei battalion bravely attacked, after two hours of fierce battle, the bandits collapsed to the northeast. The department arrived at Ge Yuan and encountered about 2,000 bandits with more than 1,000 guns, stubbornly resisting the mountain. After five hours of fierce battle, and four or five hand-to-hand combats, the bandits were unable to support themselves and collapsed to the northwest. They were also intercepted by Wang's regiment. It is estimated that more than 200 bandits were killed, more than 100 were captured alive, and many guns, spears, documents, propaganda materials, and books were seized. It was found that Ge Yuan had the Pseudo-Jiangxi Northeast Special Committee Cadre School and the Normal School and the Hengfeng County Soviet Red Regiment.

Page 10

The agencies are indeed the bases of Fang Shao. Troops are currently being dispatched to search and suppress in the surrounding areas to completely clear them. I respectfully report this, Ruan Zhaochang Jian Yin."

The Korean Border Gradually Returns to Peace, Overseas Chinese in Andong Scatter

▲ Some Return to Korea, Some Return to Their Hometowns

Andong Express News, Since the Korean Anti-Chinese incident occurred, the number of overseas Chinese who fled to this area was statistically about 3,000, excluding those who relied on relatives and friends or went to other places. In terms of food and drink, about 150 yuan per day is required. The donations from all parties were exceptionally enthusiastic. As of the afternoon of the 17th, the total donation from all circles in Andong was 13,000 yuan in current silver. All circles in Liaoning are also very concerned about this. The provincial farmers' association, the provincial labor union, the chamber of commerce, the education association, and the press association jointly initiated donations. However, fearing that there would be an urgent need for funds here, the government bank first borrowed 3,000 yuan of silver dollars and elected Zhao Yushi, the chairman of the press association, Wang Huayi, the chairman of the education association, and Lu Naigeng, the chairman of the labor union, as representatives. They took a car to Andong on the morning of the 16th, and many people went to the station to welcome them. County magistrate Wang Jiegong and Zhang Hanwei, the chief of the commercial port public security bureau, led the three representatives to the first refugee shelter (Danggui No. 1 Platform). The three representatives handed over 3,000 yuan in donations and made speeches to the refugees, saying, "First, don't forget the enemies who made the Koreans harm us. Second, don't forget the country. We must first unite and be ready to sacrifice for the country when the opportunity arises. Third, those who harm us have failed. All countries in the world know that the Japanese police have the power to protect overseas Chinese from all countries and will not allow Korean rioters to riot. This is also the Japanese side's consistent claim. If it does not admit that it instigated this Korean riot, it means that the police are not powerful enough to protect overseas Chinese. Of course, all countries will send troops to protect themselves. In this regard, they will eventually have to admit it. Wouldn't it be a failure for them?" After the speeches, they went to various shelters to express their condolences and accompanied Zhu Fu, the consul of Sinuiju, to cross the river to inspect Sinuiju for a week. They then returned to Andong. According to the three representatives, the city of Sinuiju has been pacified, and all Chinese merchants have resumed their businesses one after another. They also investigated the total number of Chinese workers employed by Japanese merchants in Sinuiju, totaling 1,100, including 150 at the Yalu River Timber Factory, 160 at the Forestry Agency, 150 at the Korean Transportation Company, 25 at the Match Company, 120 at the Showa Timber Factory, 25 at the Box Manufacturing Company, 60 at the Round-in Timber Factory, 50 at the Kondo Timber Factory, 80 at the Shibata Timber Factory, and 200 at the Oji Paper Company. At 6:00 PM, County Magistrate Wang and Director Zhang hosted a banquet for the three representatives. At 8:40, the three representatives left Andong and returned to Liaoning. All the important figures in the city went to the station to see them off. In recent days, the situation in various parts of the Korean border seems to be gradually returning to peace. Except for one or two companies in Sinuiju that have suffered too much loss and are unable to reorganize, all other companies opened their doors on the 16th and resumed business as usual. However, on the afternoon of the 16th, there were still more than 30 refugees from Pyongyang who were all from the labor sector and were immediately put into the first shelter. They claimed that the suburbs near Pyongyang are still not very stable, and because they have been severely damaged, merchants are unable to recover for a while, and most have not gone. Laborers, like startled birds, are timid and afraid, so they dare not stay there. The leaders of the local authorities have recently decided that since the Korean border is gradually returning to peace, the 3,000 refugees living in the shelter should be ordered to return to their old places to make a living or return to their hometowns. The decision was made at a meeting on the 16th to implement the repatriation. On the one hand, they negotiated with the Zhengji Company, the Qialong Taikoo Steamship Company, and the four major shipping companies to charge half the price for refugees taking ships. As a result, more than a thousand refugees have returned to Sinuiju in the past two days (this route does not require road fees), and each person is subsidized with two yuan for miscellaneous expenses. On the 17th, more than 60 people took the Taikoo Ningbo wheel to Yantai. In addition to providing ship tickets, each person was given another two yuan for miscellaneous expenses. According to calculations that night, there were only more than 1,500 refugees left, who were all merged into the three shelters of Danggui, Northeast, and Dongming. The Xinming Stage and the Dongping Cinema, which were vacated, will be opened for performances after some tidying up in a day or two. It is also heard that the Guangli ship of the Zhengji Company is scheduled to sail to Qingdao on the 19th, and it is expected to carry 400 to 500 refugees. This is because 60% of the refugees are from Rizhao County, Shandong, and need to transfer from Qingdao. Among the Chinese residents in Korea, those from Rizhao County, Shandong, have suffered the most in this incident. Because they are engaged in labor such as growing vegetable gardens in Korea, after the incident, all their miscellaneous items were lost, so they were unable to return to Korea and had no choice but to seek to return to their hometowns. It is estimated that the refugees here will be completely repatriated between the 22nd and 23rd of this month. According to news from the Sinuiju Consulate, the consulate is currently planning post-disaster plans and is conducting a survey of the number of losses in various places. Zhu Fu, the consul, followed the telegram order of the National Government's Ministry of Foreign Affairs and specially submitted a note to the Governor of Pingan North Road in Korea yesterday, reserving the right to demand compensation for losses. The full text of his note is as follows: "Regarding the note, during the Korean riots, within the jurisdiction of your governor, in addition to the one known death on Zhongzhi Island and the injured in Dayudong Yunshan Beizhen, the remaining losses are still under investigation. As for the undisturbed areas, I am deeply grateful for your governor's order to the police stations to guard and protect. However, for the loss of life and property suffered by overseas Chinese in other places due to this riot, please reserve all rights to demand compensation to be handled by our country's central government. In addition to still requesting your governor to do your best to protect and prevent the recurrence of such unfortunate events, it is appropriate to notify you. I hope you will check it out." (18th)

Wuhu Circles Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese General Assembly

▲ The Business Community Immediately Implemented Economic Severance with Japan

Wuhu Correspondence, The people of Wuhu are extremely indignant about the Wanbaoshan incident and the arbitrary massacre of overseas Chinese compatriots in Korea by the Korean government under the direction of the Japanese government. After active preparations, they convened representatives from all walks of life in Wuhu at the Star Cinema this morning to hold an Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese General Assembly. All stores, agencies, groups, and schools in the city lowered their flags to half-mast for one day to mourn the overseas Chinese who died in the disaster. When the meeting opened, more than 1,000 representatives attended. The presidium was composed of the Party Department, the Public Security Bureau, the County Government, the 171st Brigade Headquarters, and the Party Department of the 341st Regiment. Zhang Shuye, the Minister of Propaganda of the Party Department, was elected as the general chairman to report on the truth of the Wanbaoshan incident and the massacre of overseas Chinese in Korea, and to describe the atrocities committed by the Japanese against China in the past. After the report, the entire venue was silent for five minutes to express condolences. Then, Wu Xingzhou, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, and Yu Yuying, the county magistrate, delivered speeches. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Telegraph the Central Party Department and the National Government to announce the fact that Japanese imperialism instigated Koreans to cruelly kill overseas Chinese to all countries in the world and lodge the most serious protest against Japan; (2) Send a telegram to the whole country to rise up together and be the government's diplomatic backing; (3) Send a telegram to the central government to order the Ministries of Education and Interior to instruct schools and people's organizations across the country to engage in military training and unite against Japan; (4) Send a telegram to comfort the overseas Chinese who suffered in Korea; (5) Send a telegram to Commander-in-Chief Chiang to eliminate the communist bandits and reorganize the army to deal with Japan within a time limit; (6) Send a telegram to Vice Commander-in-Chief Zhang to pay attention to Japan's Manchuria and Mongolia policy and take strict precautions to safeguard national rights; (7) Organize the Wuhu Circles Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Committee to implement permanent economic severance with Japan and notify the Chamber of Commerce to immediately instruct all merchants not to order Japanese goods again, and citizens not to buy Japanese goods again. Next, the draft of the general assembly telegram and declaration was passed. The meeting adjourned at 1:00 PM, shouting slogans.

(July 21)

Local Correspondence

Fengxian

The Story of a Father Digging Out His Son's Eyes is Bizarre On the 11th of this month, Jiang Agen, a farmer in the 63rd Waizu area of the Third District, was taking a nap at home when suddenly many people came to his house and dug out his eyes. Neighbors heard the noise and rushed to help, but it was too late. Agen reported to the nearby Public Security Third Branch. On the 19th, two suspects, Wu Degen and Shao Shengtang, were arrested and brought to the bureau for interrogation. Unexpectedly, the bureau suddenly received a report from Jiang Apu, Agen's father, yesterday (the 20th), stating that his son Agen was dedicated to smoking and gambling, and his family property was exhausted. He had a wife and four children, and life was difficult. He had repeatedly warned him but he did not listen, so he was angry and did this. He repented for this period and repeatedly stated that the two people in custody, Wu and Shao, had nothing to do with it. However, Director Chen thought the matter was too bizarre and there might be other circumstances, so he transferred the three criminals to the judiciary last night (the 21st) for investigation and verification.

Songjiang

Summary of County Government Meeting The County Government held a county government meeting today (the 22nd), chaired by County Magistrate Shen, to discuss the following matters: (1) County Magistrate's motion, the property donation compilation and inspection register of the shops in this county has been submitted to the government by the Finance Bureau. There are a total of 4,269 shops in the county, with a total monthly rent of 19,425 yuan and one dime. 10% should be collected, and the monthly donation is 1,942 yuan, five jiao, and one fen. Please decide when to start collecting the money. The motion was resolved that the County Government would convene the heads of the Public Security Bureau, the Finance Bureau, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, and the chiefs of each district to discuss again on a scheduled basis. (2) County Magistrate's motion, the houses in this government are old and dilapidated, and they are all tilted. Recently, there has been too much mold and rain, and the passageway between the Great Hall and the Second Hall has collapsed. How should we raise funds for repairs? It was resolved that the county would order craftsmen to estimate the repairs.

He appointed Qiang Dunbao as the chief of the General Affairs Section, Feng Gengbai as the chief of the Collection Section, and Wu Yuanhou as the director of miscellaneous taxes. Suzhou

Communist Bandit from Wujin Surrenders and is Escorted to Suzhou After the communist bandit Wu Yinzhai was reported by someone in his hometown of Wujin, he surrendered to the county government. Yesterday (the 22nd), he was interrogated by the Bandit Suppression Command in Suzhou.

Ordered to Dissolve the Sedan Chair Carriers Union The sedan chair carriers union in Suzhou has long been organized and established, but the county government received instructions from the Construction Department yesterday, based on the order of the Ministry of Industry, stating that there is no direct relationship between rickshaw pullers and sedan chair carriers, and there is no need to organize a union. It should be dissolved, etc. The county government immediately forwarded the order to comply.

Bandit Suppression Department Executes Two Kidnappers The kidnappers Dong Daotang were direct uncles and nephews from Hefei. They committed many crimes in Wujiang and other places. They were captured by the Taihu Bandit Suppression Command, interrogated, and found guilty. They were sentenced to death and approved by the provincial government. At 10:00 AM on the 22nd, the two criminals were tied to the Wangshudun execution ground and executed by shooting.

Changshu

Fushan Songqi Harbor Soldiers and Bandits Open Fire - At approximately 4:00 AM on the 19th, the residence of farmer Yang Xiaoyu in Yangjiazhaiji, Babao, about three miles from Fushan town, was suddenly raided by a gang of over ten bandits armed with many guns. They arrived in a fast boat, landed at the local harbor, and seized Xiaoyu's daughter, Fengfeng (18 years old), grandson Jiajia (only 6 years old), nephew Pingping (7 years old), and Xiaoyu himself (54 years old),

taking them all away together. They took them to the Haikou of Hujing Harbor and boarded the bandit boat to leave. Unexpectedly, when they reached Songji Harbor in Chongming Sha, they encountered a Zhenyu patrol warship stationed in Hu, which was patrolling the area. Seeing the suspicious behavior of the boat, the gunnery officer Ji Congchun ordered them to be inspected. Unexpectedly, the boat continued to speed away, trying to escape. At a distance of about 400 meters, the warship fired a warning shot. The bandit boat approached the beach, and they retaliated with weapons. The two sides engaged in a fierce battle for about two hours. The bandits gradually lost ground and fled towards the beach. Two bandits were shot and killed. Seeing that the bandits had gone far away, the warship soldiers searched the boat and found the four hostages, Yang Xiaoyu and others, tied up. However, the hostages were pale with fear. They were rescued onto the warship one by one. The warship soldiers also found a rifle and twenty-four bullets on the bandit boat. Subsequently, Officer Ji Congchun hired a small boat and sent the hostages to the headquarters of the 13th Water Police Team in the city overnight. The hostages are currently staying at the team headquarters, waiting to be notified to their families to come and pick them up.

The Trial Officer Accuses the Party Committee - The former trial officer of Changshu, Gu Yushang, was previously involved in an incident where his wife, Fei Guoying, was allegedly seduced and eloped by the secretary, which has attracted considerable public attention. However, while Gu was in office in Changshu, he handled a murder case outside the West Gate and clashed with the Party Committee member Shen Zuguang. Gu then suspected Shen of obstructing official duties and interfering with the judiciary, so he resigned from his post at the High Court and filed a lawsuit with the High Court. Initially, because Shen was a Party Committee member, it was feared that the same-level government would be biased in the trial, so he requested that the case be transferred to the Wudi Court for trial. Three months have passed since the judge read the case, but there has been no summons for a court hearing. Recently, news was received that the High Court has made a ruling on this case, the gist of which is roughly: "The County Party Committee and the County Government are not subordinate institutions, and the Party Committee member is not a public official. You can file a complaint with the County Government where the defendant is located, without specifying a court for trial." Now, after receiving the approval, Gu will come to Changshu again to file a complaint with the county.

Wuxi

Doctor's House Robbery Case Solved - At 5:00 AM on the 9th of this month, the residence of Jiangbei doctor Wang Daoan in the Dalou Lane, behind the old Yizhuang of the Qin family in the city, was robbed by four bandits, resulting in a loss of over 700 yuan. It is now known that the day before yesterday afternoon, Captain Xue received a report from an informant that the perpetrators of this case were hiding in the Xiaoshadu area of Shanghai. Upon receiving the report, Captain Xue immediately led detectives Dai Shouquan, Luo Shaoqing, and others by car to Shanghai to arrest them at the address. One bandit was captured on the spot and escorted to Wuxi for interrogation. The suspect confessed his name as Zhou Xinshun, nicknamed "Little Blind Man," 25 years old, from Zhouzhuang, Funing, Jiangbei. He confessed to the robbery of Dr. Wang's house, but stated that the leaders of the case were Qian and two others (the secret code for the bandit leader), who had three pistols. He claimed he was invited by them and received 13 yuan in spoils and a gold ring. The leader lived outside the South Gate, near the Dagong Bridge. Based on the confession, Captain Xue summoned detectives and officers, together with Wu Zhengrong, the chief of political affairs police, and took the suspect Zhou by boat to capture the others outside the South Gate. They were indeed arrested two suspected bandit men and women in the first workshop of the Yisheng Silk Factory, No. 12 Yaoyaowanhoubeixiang, and three pistols and twenty rounds of ammunition were found. They were immediately taken to the boat and escorted to the Public Security Bureau. They reported to Director Xu and continued to cooperate in apprehending the remaining bandits. At the same time, one of the main bandits involved in the robbery of a tailor shop under Huishang Bridge outside Guangfu Gate was arrested and sent to the Public Security Bureau for questioning yesterday.

Zhenjiang

Court Tried Major Gambling Case Yesterday - Wu Baozhi, a partner in Shengtai Hardware Store, lost over 2,400 yuan in gambling after being cheated. He gambled 18 times with over 50 people, of whom only 41 were known. As a result, he embezzled 2,000 yuan from the company's account. The shop owner discovered the embezzlement and sued him in court for embezzlement. He has already been sentenced to six months in prison and fined 300 yuan. Upon hearing the news, his family hired lawyer Yang Puzhen to sue Zhang Yucheng, Wu Xianbin, and 41 others in court for colluding to gamble and defraud. The court accepted the case and scheduled to investigate separately on the 3 days. It was reported that only Wu Xianbin reported yesterday, and the others did not. It was not until after noon that the Prosecutor's Office opened a court session and questioned Wu. Wu was ordered to post bail and await further questioning. According to Wu's wife, Chen, Wu gambled 18 times, and there was a list of all of them which has been submitted to the court. Zhang Yucheng hosted the first game in Shuangjing Lane, and Wu lost the most, amounting to over 1,000 yuan. The rest were lost in smaller amounts. It is reported that many of the 41 people summoned had their names misspelled, resulting in their refusal to accept the summons. It is said that only over 20 people received them, and over ten were returned because they were not in Zhenjiang or the names were incorrect.

Yangzhou

Consult the Provincial Government to Speed Up the Construction of Long-Distance Telephones - Zhang Zhijiang, the Pacification Commissioner, considering that the Provincial Government planned to build state-owned long-distance telephones, yesterday (20th) specially consulted the Provincial Government, requesting that the Construction Department speed up the construction and provide a map of the routes across the province in advance, to facilitate the work of suppressing bandits.

Pawnbrokers Request Shortened Redemption Period - Dexin, Fucheng, and Dunji Pawnshops, noting that there are only three pawnshops in the city and their operating costs are relatively high, submitted a report to the County Government outlining their difficulties and requesting that the redemption period be shortened to twelve months to facilitate financial circulation. Yesterday, the County Government forwarded the request to the Construction Department.

Child Missing After Being Washed Away by Waves - The water level in the upper reaches of the Grand Canal has been rising daily. It was first reported that the water level at the Sangu Gate Zhichun rose continuously from the 15th to one zhang, eight chi, and one cun. While the residents along the embankment were in a state of fear day and night, two ships, Yongchang and Xintai Zhou, sailed down from Qingjiang, reaching Baoying. The waves from the ships overturned the dining table in front of a resident's house, and a child went missing. The public frantically chased after the ship and seized the Xintai Zhou, unloading its machinery, injuring the ship's crew, and detaining it for negotiation. They also reported the matter for investigation. The Yongchang ship, fortunately being a fast ship, managed to escape.

Hangzhou

Old Woman Killed by Snake Around Neck - Chen, the wife of Lou Shixiang in Gudalou, Liuxia Town, Hang County, who was in her sixties, went to the grassland to fetch mulberry branches for cooking the evening meal the day before yesterday. Suddenly, a venomous snake flew out of the firewood pile and coiled around Chen's neck, tightening its grip. She tragically died. When someone saw it and reported it to Lou, the snake was still coiled around her neck. This kind of tragic death is truly unheard of. Her family has prepared a coffin for her burial.

Letters

Letter from Juegang Hua Feng Reclamation Company

To the Editor,

Having read the article on p.13, titled "Forced Opening of Dikes and Shooting Farmers", we find that it is the exact opposite of what happened. We have checked with the company's reclaimed land and found that it is located in the low-lying area of the Laoyu and has been heavily invested in by the company for dredging rivers, building fences, and creating gates. The Laoyu has its own outlet for water. In this instance, the people of Laoyu disregard the interests of others and gathered the Bao Wei Tuan to force the opening of the company's North Park in order to swiftly remove water. The company's farmers were outnumbered and did not retaliate. No farmers were killed or injured. The facts are clearly on record. The company's reclaimed land was affected by the disaster and the farmers suffered greatly. We are currently negotiating the matter based on reason and request that it be corrected to publicize the facts.

Signed, Juegang Hua Feng Reclamation Company.

Educational News

Highlights

Curriculum Standards for Primary and Secondary Schools Have Been Set

▲Secondary School Curriculum Standards Also Completed Yesterday

丨Entrance Examinations for University Freshmen and Teacher Training Must Be Based on Standards丨

Nanjing, 22nd - The Curriculum and Equipment Committee for Primary and Secondary Schools held a general meeting on the 22nd. The curriculum standards for secondary schools have also been completed. After being organized, they will be submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval and will be announced before August 20th. Key points: (1) The goal of craft courses in junior high school is to cultivate the concept that all occupations are equal and to provide necessary craft skills for life. (2) The Party Ideology course will be submitted to the Standing Committee of the Central Committee for review. (3) The syllabus for junior high school history textbooks was approved. (4) The goal of physical education in junior high school is to cultivate healthy recreational habits. Wushu and Guoshu will be collectively referred to as Guoshu. Physical education in senior high school will be passed according to the review plan. (5) The music curriculum will be submitted to Xiao Youmei for revision. (6) All other subjects will follow the interim curriculum standards. (7) Elective courses in senior high school must have at least 15 students to open a class. If a single grade has fewer than 40 students, a class can be opened with at least 10 students. (8) The Ministry of Education is requested to issue a notice to all universities that the questions for entrance examinations must be based on the curriculum standards. A further notice will be issued to all universities and education departments in provinces and cities to pay attention to the training of primary and secondary school teachers based on the curriculum standards.

丨Details of the Second Day of the Primary School Group丨

The primary school group held a group review meeting in the morning of the 21st and a general meeting in the afternoon. All courses for kindergartens and primary schools were compiled separately. The organization and textual revision of all courses will be the responsibility of the Ministry of Education. It has been limited to the ministry to announce it before August 20th. The meeting was chaired by Wu Yan, and the following resolutions were made: (1) The Chinese, social studies, and health courses were all revised and passed according to the original review plan. (2) The music requirements were increased by three items: one time for the primary level and two times for the advanced level. Regarding the issue of singing in unison, opinions from experts will be sought before a decision is made. (3) In the general outline, (A) the overall goals were deleted, and the item "cultivate a scientific attitude" was added. "Scientific knowledge and skills" was changed to "knowledge and skills for life." (B) Item 2 of the scope of work was deleted. (C) Group activity time, the names of various group activities were deleted for high, middle, and low levels.

丨Details of the First Day of the Middle School Group丨

The secondary school group held a plenary meeting in the morning of the 21st, attended by Hu Huanyong, Ren Mengxian, Sun Liangong, Zhang Guoren, Xia Chengfeng, Cheng Qibao (Xia Dai), Zhong Daoxuan, Gu Shusen, Zhao Zhengduo, Lin Duanfu, Xu Zhunqi, Dai Yingguan, Xu Yiqiao, Zhang Shiyi, Zheng Tonghe, Zhu Baoqin, Yao Wencai, Zhao NaiChuan, Du Tingxiu, Xie Shuying, Li Qingsong. The meeting was chaired by Gu Shusen and recorded by Weng Zhida. The meeting began with ceremonial procedures, and the chairman reported on the progress of the Ministry of Education in organizing the review of the curriculum standards for each subject, as well as the agenda for this meeting. Discussion items: General review opinions for each subject in junior and senior high school. (1) Chinese: Xu Xuefen's points should be stipulated in accordance with the resolution of the previous meeting. The rest should be revised based on the interim curriculum standards and the general review opinions submitted by the group members. (2) English: Except for the credit hours, which should be modified in accordance with the resolution of the previous meeting, and the correction of printing errors, the rest will be passed according to the original proposed interim standards. (3) Nature: The departmental system and the mixed system coexist. Regarding the departmental system, except for one course, "General Idea of Natural Phenomena," which will be moved to the second semester of the third year, mineralogy will be taught in chemistry according to the original standard and will not be set up as a separate course. The arrangement of other courses and the distribution of time will be included in the overall timetable. Geography courses will be taught every semester, with credits given. Chinese geography will be taught in the second year of junior high school with six credits. Foreign geography will be included in the second semester of the third year with three credits. (B) Eight items in the syllabus for senior high school geography will be changed. 1. will be changed to "The Status of Water, Land, and Air Transportation in Our Country." 14. will be changed to "National Defense Issues." 1. "Our Country's National Defense." 2. "The Current Situation of Our Country's Land, Sea, and Air Forces." 3. "Comparison of Our Country's Land, Sea, and Air Forces with Those of Major Powers." 15. The aviation issue will be completely deleted. 16. will be changed to 15 in sequence. (D) The rest will be passed according to the general review opinions. (7) Arithmetic: Pass according to the review plan.

Ministry Orders the Acceptance and Examination of Students in Beiping Who Have Already Been Screened

The Ministry of Education has announced that students from unregistered and closed private colleges and above in Beiping who have already been screened may be accepted and examined by various schools and allowed to transfer to the final year of study. This has been communicated to the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities, as well as national universities, colleges, and vocational schools. The results of the screening examinations for graduates and students of unregistered and closed private colleges and above held this year in Beiping have been reported by the Beiping Municipal Education Bureau. The Ministry has reviewed the results in detail and found them to be satisfactory. All students who have passed and been downgraded have been issued transfer certificates by the Ministry, ordering them to apply to public or registered private colleges and above. Those graduates with better grades may transfer to the final year of study when the schools are recruiting, without being restricted by Article 4 of the University Regulations and Article 4 of the Amended Vocational School Regulations. In addition to distributing the notice, the Ministry hereby orders that the Department forward it to provincial and registered colleges and above.
