Free Talk

A Word of Advice

— Zui Chi Sheng

▲Few words prevent idle chatter. Quiet cultivation leads to longevity.

▲Meeting high officials and nobles is not as good as talking to peddlers and vendors.

▲When doing things, one should think one step further. When in a situation, one should think one step back.

▲People only know how to keep themselves clean, but do not know how to cleanse their hearts. Therefore, there are many base and filthy people in the world.

▲We live in this troubled world. Even if we cannot be optimistic, we should be philosophical.

▲Money and spirit should not be wasted. Waste leads to ruin.

▲If everyone could understand the true meaning of the saying "How many years can one live to be a hundred?", countless disputes would be avoided in the world.

▲Fear of difficulty and complacency are obstacles to all undertakings.

▲Why are there so many male statues and no female statues?

▲Although the male is good at killing, sometimes it is no match for the power of the female.

▲When young people's blood is not yet settled and their foundation is not yet established, they want to embark on the road of love. The danger is not only falling down.

▲"When rich and noble, relatives are in awe" is the snobbish attitude of the ancients. However, in today's society, "rich and noble" should be replaced by "poor and lowly."

▲It is advisable to look ahead and behind in everything. Unexpectedly, the law also commits the fault of "looking ahead but not behind." (A lawyer surnamed Ren was accused by his wife of sodomy. The prosecutor dismissed the case. The reason is that the law has no clear provisions on whether the anus should be entered.)

The Perils of Siberian Travel (Part 1)

— Ping

Mr. Cao Zhongyuan, who studied radio science in Germany, traveled from Germany to Japan this time, passing through Siberia and arriving in Shanghai via Manchuria. He is currently waiting for a ship to cross the East Sea to continue his investigation and research. Yesterday, he told reporters about the perilous situation on the way to Siberia, which shows the economic panic and domestic disorder in Soviet Russia. I will now classify and summarize it as follows.

▲Ruble Oddities – The economic situation in Russia, due to its low international status, has caused the ruble's market value to plummet. In Berlin, one mark can be exchanged for more than fifteen rubles. One US dollar can be exchanged for more than fifty rubles. In Manchuria, one Chinese currency yuan can also be exchanged for twelve rubles. When a traveler enters Russian territory, customs officials conduct extremely strict searches, prohibiting the carrying of foreign currency. They must also exchange Russian currency at the exchange offices attached to the stations. However, the money that travelers carry with them is mostly British pounds or US dollars. In Russia, each US dollar is only exchanged for 1.94 rubles. If the remaining rubles are converted into US dollars when leaving the country, two rubles are converted into one US dollar. The disorder of the exchange rate is such.

▲Soaring Ticket Prices – The ticket price of the international Liche train on the Siberian Railway was increased by one-half by Soviet Russia without authorization in August of last year. It was increased by 25% in March of this year. It was increased by another 25% starting in June. In less than a year, it has increased tenfold. However, the ticket prices for China, Germany, and Poland remain the same. This has now aroused protests from all parties. The negotiations are being handled, but Russia has not given a concrete answer. Furthermore, Chinese travelers must pay an additional telegraph fee of 25 marks per person before their passports are signed, which is also a strange thing.

▲Restrictions on Expenses – Travelers, regardless of whether they are in hard or soft berths (that is, the difference between third-class and first and second-class cars), can pre-purchase meal tickets, worth US$23.10. They can only be used for seven days in Russia. According to the new regulations of Soviet Russia, each person must spend at least 7.5 rubles or US$3.87 per day during these seven days, for a total of more than US$27 in seven days. In addition to buying meal tickets, if this amount is not used up, it will be deducted by the customs officials when leaving the country after inspection and calculation. Several students traveling with Mr. Cao had their remaining money confiscated by the Red Russian customs officers, without any reason being announced. They do not care about travelers lacking funds.

▲Equipment in the Car – Third-class cars require a separate rental for berths. A thin mat is used as a mattress. A tablecloth is used as a blanket. It costs US$1.50 for every three nights. The swaying is very painful. In the summer, dust and sand fly. If you open the window, the air is dirty. If you close the window, it is stuffy and hot. There is no bathroom. There is only boiling water for washing. The color is scorched yellow, half mixed with sand and soil. It is directly discharged from the locomotive. There is no doctor. The conductor and attendants all have fierce faces and are not dressed neatly. And no one can speak English, German, or French. It is very inconvenient to communicate.

A Record of What I Saw at the Jiangyin Garden Hotel

— Yu Bai

Last year, I passed through Jiangyin and stayed at the Garden Hotel in Liu Ling Lane, South Gate. The name "Garden" is truly worthy of the name here. This place is a large and beautiful garden, called Yi Yuan. It was built by Grand Scribe Zhu, a former Qing Dynasty scholar. A part of the room was opened as a hotel, not intended to make a profit, but to make friends with the world. The layout of the garden is both elegant and neat, making people linger and unwilling to leave. There is a couplet hanging in the hall, elegant and neat. I will record it here for the public to enjoy. "In troubled times, do not worry too much. Let him be a viper or a snake. Just wander in Zhu's Yi Yuan, be content with your lot, and sell yourself for eternity." A floating life should indulge in wine, do not ask about slaying the dragon dog. And walk into Liu Ling's old lane. When you have nothing to do, I advise you to have another cup." There is a talking parrot in the garden that is good at calling "Huang Bao Che" (rickshaw), which is clear and crisp to hear. There is also a green-haired turtle, supplied in a pot. From a distance, it looks like lush green grass, emerald green. To this day, I do not know if it still exists.

Musk Deer Milk

— Xiao Chang

The musk deer is similar to a deer but smaller, without horns, and its fur is brownish-yellow. Its milk is extremely nutritious, surpassing cow and goat milk. In western Zhejiang, such as Hangzhou, Yuyao, Wu'an, etc., many people use it as a tonic. However, the method of obtaining milk is not like squeezing it from the nipples of cows and goats, but taking it from the stomach of a small musk deer. Therefore, to obtain musk deer milk, one must first capture a small musk deer. I will now record the capture of small musk deer and the extraction of milk as follows.

Musk deer live in the mountains and forests in autumn and winter, and in the marshes in spring and summer. Every year around the time of Xiaoman (Minor Full), is their childbearing period. Each litter usually has three or four offspring. They are often born in the shallow grass at the foot of mountains or in flat marshy grasslands (without water). People who capture small musk deer to obtain musk deer milk usually go to the mountains and marshes after Xiaoman, with companions holding sticks to search through the grass. If they catch one, they immediately kill it. And dig out its stomach. Or sell it to others on the spot, or take it back and take out its milk. Put it in a cloth and press it to dry. Wrap it in bamboo shoots and place it next to you to allow it to absorb human energy. Then sell it gradually. Its value is expensive. Each tael (ounce) requires about twenty silver dollars.

The reason why the small musk deer is killed immediately after being caught is that after being caught, it often spits out the milk in its stomach, or cries out loudly. When it cries out, its milk is digested with the sound. This is probably the same as when a musk deer is caught, it immediately tears its musk gland with its claws.

Capturing small musk deer is not easy. Both the old and small musk deer are extremely clever. After the small musk deer are born, the old musk deer will hide each small musk deer in different places. The positions in which they are hidden may form a square or a triangle. And each musk deer must be moved once a day. And the distance between each musk deer is moved farther and farther. When they are first born, the places where each musk deer is hidden are only a few steps apart. Afterwards, they gradually move away, up to about a mile. The reason why the old musk deer does this is that, firstly, it is easier to remember when breastfeeding. The old musk deer only breastfeeds one offspring a day, rotating in a cycle. Secondly, to prevent being wiped out in one fell swoop when an enemy attacks. As for the small musk deer, they are also very cunning. They hide in the grass all day long. People do not move when they reach them. Even if they are trampled to death, they do not make a sound. They must wait for the capturer to reach out and urge them before they jump and flee. Sometimes they immerse themselves in the water, slightly revealing their mouths and noses on the surface of the water, covered with algae to avoid human eyes. Therefore, capturers often miss them.

Once a small musk deer drinks water from the Xia Zhi (Summer Solstice), its feet will have strength and it will be able to escape far when encountering an enemy, so it is not easy to catch at this time. In fact, small musk deer can eat tender grass slightly by the time of the Summer Solstice, so their feet are stronger.

Obtaining a small musk deer is a fortunate thing. But there is still good luck and bad luck among them. The acquired are divided into empty stomach and full stomach. Those with an empty stomach have not been breastfed for two or three days. The milk in the stomach has been almost completely digested. Those with a full stomach have just been breastfed last night. The stomach is full of milk. The one with the most milk can get two or three taels (ounces) after being dried, worth about thirty or forty silver dollars. Those who get it are indeed lucky.

Musk deer milk produced in Wukang is the best. Those who know how to identify it can tell. The county has a musk deer milk shop that buys and sells for customers to earn commissions. This thing has the fastest effect when babies take it. All thin and weak babies can become fat, white, and lovely within a month after taking it.

A Record of Divine Art

— Ke Ding'an

Mr. Huang Hanhous of Jiangdu is an elegant gentleman who is skilled in calligraphy. He has studied all the schools of Jin and Tang. He is especially good at carving bamboo fans. He can carve the full text of the Sacred Teachings Preface, the Thirteen Prefaces of the Orchid Pavilion, etc., in a space no more than six inches long and no more than five minutes wide. The strokes are clear and the spirit is full. They are not bad at all compared to the original posts. Recently, he has been sought after by many people and has specially opened an exhibition at the Ningbo Fellow Association for the enjoyment of enthusiasts. Among his works, such as the full text of Yan Zhenqing's contention for seats, the full text of Huai Ren's collection of Wang Youjun's calligraphy Heart Sutra, Zhu Zhishan's calligraphy of Du Fu's Eight Autumn Exhortations, Su Dongpo's Treatise on Health Preservation, the Former and Latter Chibi Fu, and the calligraphy of Emperor Taizong of Tang, Wang Youjun, Wang Xianzhi, and Huang Shangu are all vividly carved and can be called masterpieces. I heard from Hanhou that he has liked carving bamboo since he was twenty years old. At first, he still felt it was difficult, and he always felt inconvenient when playing the knife. After careful study, he suddenly felt refreshed. And he can do whatever he wants without any obstacles. For example, when carving a fan, he only needs to mark the number of lines on the fan bone with ink, and then he can play the knife and get what he wants. Qingshan Nong praised it as a divine art, which is indeed appropriate. The smallest words cannot be distinguished by eyesight. You must observe them with a microscope to see them all. I asked if his eyesight was damaged. According to him, his eyesight is better. This is really amazing. Hanhou is only thirty years old, and what he has achieved is already amazing. How can the rapid progress he will make in the future be limited?

Travels in India (Sixty-Six)

— Ling Hua

On the morning of the 28th, many young students came and were willing to teach me Hindi. They also wanted to learn Chinese. The children's smiles were lovely. Their intentions were very sincere. Their English was still struggling. I was very moved. Principal Nalun Misha wished that I would live in Benares and not return to China. How much the Indians love the Chinese. The Principal does not harm birds. I live in this room. The doors and windows are wide open. Sometimes the food is placed on the table, and the birds come first. I also do not feel annoyed. I heard that in Tibet, when people die, they are abandoned in the wild for birds and beasts to eat. Think about it, the human body still has a day when it is eaten by birds. How about rice grains? Wonderful. Indians can live in groups with birds and beasts. There are no meat eaters in Indian schools. All are vegetarians. It is said that if there are those who do not eat vegetarian food, they are excluded from the school. According to reports, Indians are strong and great in body. This proves that eating meat is just a habit and superstition. In fact, it is of no benefit to life. I have written many health books. I have been a vegetarian for seventeen years since my mother died. My spirit is more than that of ordinary people. This is enough to prove it.

On this day, four classes of students from the Indian school held a graduation ceremony. I was invited to attend and give a speech. The time was very long. From 10:00 AM to 3:00 PM. I only attended at 12:00, which already felt too long. Music was interspersed in the middle. One person played the drums. One person sang and sang with a small harmonium. I do not know what the words were. The students all laughed. Art was also added in the middle. It was the breathing technique of those who practiced inner work. China and Japan both imitate this meditation. India is the true ancestral master. A woman playing the piano is drawn on the students' diplomas. It is said that she is the goddess of art. The students received their diplomas and performed a ritual of touching the feet and then touching their own heads to the Principal and the teachers. It is a simplified version of the foot-touching ritual mentioned in Buddhist scriptures. It is reminiscent of ancient customs. It is not like the school spirit of China, which emphasizes equality. After receiving their diplomas, the students also transferred various souvenirs to the school teachers. There were mirrors, portraits of famous people, etc. They were all placed on the altar. Flower wreaths were also hung on the necks of the teachers. Students wore wreaths when receiving their diplomas. The Principal personally put them on. The teachers and students were courteous to each other. It makes people think that there is no country in the world that respects teachers as much as India. Because I have given several speeches here, I was also given a flower wreath. The wreath was made of flowers. There are flowers everywhere in India. The rituals of burning incense, scattering flowers, and applying fragrance were also performed. The incense burner placed incense in a copper plate and walked around in front of everyone. The flower scatterer scattered flower petals. The fragrance applier applied fragrant oil to everyone's foreheads. There are colors. Students applied red. Teachers applied yellow. When I came here, I realized what the Buddhist scriptures said. Everything was confirmed. Several of the top students gave speeches. My speech was about the relationship between Chinese and Indian culture. Although Chinese Buddhism cannot create its own, it is good at developing it. Although Indian Buddhism is extinct, it relies on China to promote it in East Asia and the world. The meeting was dismissed at 4:00 PM and photos were taken.

Rotary Club Novel

？？？(30)

— Xu Zhuodai

At this time, Ziliang had already returned to the room and was listening to his wife's reprimand. His wife also sat up and continued her words:

"Do you think I was asleep when I closed my eyes? I was testing your heart: I didn't expect you to abandon me and go to the back. You are so heartless! If I died today, you should be by the corpse's side until dawn, let alone that I am not dead!"

At this time, Ziliang finally came up with a defense:

"I didn't go anywhere, because I heard the maid in the kitchen washing the pot very loudly, and I was afraid of waking you up, so I planned to go downstairs and tell her."

"If that's the case, you have good intentions!"

Ziliang nodded.

"Good intentions are fine."

She paused, and Ziliang felt like a prisoner who had been pardoned, and he was relieved at once.

"However, you are still too negligent. I am sleeping in bed, how can you walk away?"

Ziliang's heart jumped again.

"I want to punish you!"

Just saying "punish," I don't know what she will punish him with. Ziliang will always be able to do it as long as he doesn't lose face in front of everyone.

"When I closed my eyes just now, I felt there were bedbugs under the pillow on this bed. Catch them for me!"

After saying that, she got out of bed.

"Catch bedbugs? I can't."

Financial Gold Bar: Initial Rise Followed by Decline

Yarn and Cotton: Chinese Yarn Experiences Smooth Sales

▲ Tomorrow, Yarn and Cloth Market Open for Half a Day

The yarn market remains flat, with no signs of revitalization. However, the overall trend is unusually stable, as the patriotic movement is becoming increasingly intense. Places like Jiangsu and Zhejiang have already inspected inferior goods and are not allowing them to pass through, creating a heated situation. Therefore, the sales of yarn from our factory have suddenly shown a thriving trend. The shipment of fine yarn is too small and insufficient to meet demand, so prices have only risen and not fallen. However, the price of Japanese goods is more sluggish, seemingly already affected. Due to slow sales of coarse yarn, large firms are selling off futures yarn, making it difficult to raise prices for the time being. However, outsiders and retail investors see the boycott movement and are unanimously inclined to buy in and go long. Tomorrow morning, the market will be closed for half a day to mourn the overseas Chinese who died, and will resume normal trading in the afternoon.

Yarn, Cotton, and Cloth Turn Weak Again

▲ American Cotton Southern Hedging: Yesterday, American cotton was weak due to a lack of significant buyers, combined with sales from the South and good harvest conditions. Futures contracts fell by 24 to 29 points, spot prices fell by 25 points. British cotton futures rose by 11 points, spot prices rose by 8 points. Egyptian cotton spot prices rose by 5 points. Indian cotton initially rose with American cotton, but later softened due to profit-taking by long positions. Nagpur fell by 1 rupee, Oomra rose by 2.75 rupees, and Broach rose by 0.75 rupees. ▲ Osaka Spot Yarn Falls 3 to 4 Yuan: Yesterday's Osaka spot yarn telegram: 20s Blue Fish 140 yuan, down 4 yuan, converted to Shanghai Standard 230 taels. 20s Red God of Wealth 133 yuan, down 4 yuan, converted to Shanghai Standard 218.5 taels. 16s Fukushima 128 yuan, down 3 yuan, converted to Shanghai Standard 210.2 taels. 16s Three Horses 128 yuan, down 3 yuan, converted to Shanghai Standard 210.2 taels.

Grains: Riverbed Rice Market Moving Upward

▲ New Gate: Yesterday, there were not many sources from various routes, as merchants suffered significant losses after the previous two days of massive price declines in this port. The initial route followed the downturn in the Shanghai market, but then turned firm due to inquiries from the 客帮, reducing the number of rice boats transporting to Shanghai. In the morning, the street trade was still good, and 苏常 thick japonica rice was the most active, with prices rising by nearly a 角. Early and late japonica rice arrived sparsely, and prices also increased by about a 角. 洋杜 glutinous rice sales were slightly tight, and glutinous rice sales were steady.

▲ South Head: Yesterday, there were still not many sources from various gangs. City and rural store sales were lively due to the morning drizzle and news of price increases in the Northern Market, causing sentiment to rise. As a result, fresh 料 thick japonica rice felt quite active. Seeing this situation, boat owners all resold, immediately raising prices by 1 or 2 角. Thin rice still arrived sporadically, and although Ning sales were sluggish, the street sales were quite high and closely linked, and the market price also increased by a 角. The market price was still healthy even though 洋杜 glutinous rice sales were not smooth, but it was still healthy because of the lack of goods. The 隂化 arrivals were sparse and the market was flat. 元元 was nimble and showed a stable trend.

Italian Raw Silk Prices Fall by More Than 10 Lire

After Italian raw silk entered the Milan market, European and American silk sales once showed upward momentum. Since entering the summer, however, the weather in ports such as New York and Marseille has been unusually hot, and silk weaving factories have stopped work. Coupled with the German economic panic, overseas silk sales have stagnated, and silk prices have fallen sharply. Double Extra Grade is only opening at 385 lire per kilo, Special Grade is 332 lire, and Superior Grade is 280 lire, each falling by more than 10 lire.

Foreign Firm Silk Sales Face Difficulties

Silk weaving factories in New York and other places are still on summer vacation, silk sales are stagnant, and telegrams have not yet turned to Shanghai. Yesterday, only Jardine Matheson, and others imported 20 bales of 黄厂 warp silk, and Meade & Company and others imported 20 bales of 黄组 warp silk. Prices remain stable.

Needle-Like Eyebrow Green Tea Sees Brisk Sales in England

Yesterday, in the foreign firm tea market in this port, Jardine Matheson, a British firm, once again made large-scale purchases of needle-like eyebrow green tea from Wuyuan and Tunxi. Xiehe, Tianxiang, Yongxing, and other firms also scrambled to handle transactions, and trading was quite robust, with the market feeling firm. The markets for Precious Eyebrow tea remained sluggish. British and French firms still held price-suppression ideas, and Chinese tea merchants' firmness varied, making it difficult to stabilize the market. Gongxi green tea, Russian firms have not yet scheduled their opening, and there are no major sales for Baitaichuang tea, making it difficult to be optimistic about the overall trend.

Flour: Inland Gang's Appetite Grows Stronger

Yesterday, the flour market showed a bullish trend, with foreign wheat prices reporting that the near-term wheat in Chicago was up $0.05, and the rest were up about $0.02. The weather was also not stable, with intermittent showers. The mainland gangs became increasingly eager. Inevitable natural disasters led to enthusiastic purchasing by buyers. In each trade, the mainland gangs were buying in, and speculative buyers were also trying hard to get in. However, the Tianjin gang took the opportunity to sell because of the current situation. Otherwise, the increase would have been even more considerable. As a result, this month's contract was up 0.0075 compared to the day before, August's was up 0.005, September and October's were up 0.01, and November and December's were up 0.015. Also, on the 23rd, in memory of the overseas Chinese, the flour market was closed for the entire day.

Distant-Term Wheat Sees Sharp Decline

Yesterday, the wheat futures market saw the early market remain bullish with foreign wheat prices. Sentiment was still stable for each month, but buyers were very quiet, and selling pressure was strong, showing a slightly sluggish market trend. By the afternoon opening, distant-term sentiment suddenly shook. This was because 7,000 tons of 四兩一錢半 Australian wheat for September and October shipment were confirmed, with 中华 factory accounting for 3,500 tons and a certain miscellaneous grain firm accounting for 3,500 tons. Once this was confirmed, they naturally sold to the market with all their might, so the distant-term decline was very sharp. Therefore, if the mainland gangs are ignorant of the foreign situation and purely based their decisions on the domestic background, there will ultimately be problems in the future. As a result, this month's and August and September's contracts were down slightly by $0.02, October's was down $0.06, and November and December's were down $0.05. The spot wheat market remained stable. Factory demand was neither too close nor too far. 3,850 bales of Yangzhou, Puzhen, Penglai, Zhoupu, Shuangfeng, Zhitang, Kunshan, Anting, Wusong, Huangdu, and Jiading wheat were opened and handled by factories such as Fuxin, Huafeng, Fufeng, and Xinda. Also, 70 bales of sample goods of Russian wheat have also opened, with a price of 3.8 taels.

North and South Goods: Fresh Zhangzhou Dried Lychees Arrive

The first batch of new 兰竹枝 and 乌叶枝 lychees produced in Zhangzhou were shipped on the Taikoo Company's Taiyuan wheel the day before yesterday. It is reported that there are a total of 888 boxes, of which hundreds of boxes are transferred to Hangzhou and other places. Each firm handles approximately 400 boxes themselves, and company goods account for less than 400 boxes. Samples were seen yesterday, the color is good, and the texture is slightly soft, but compared to previous years, they are definitely dry. Approximately 200 pieces of various brand 兰竹枝 were immediately opened at $50 taels for the best grade, $40 taels for 高乌叶, and the next best grades were reduced by $1-3 taels, market atmosphere was flat.

Sugar Market: Dumping of Medium Grade White Sugar, Market Flat

▲ Taikoo Sugar Sales Quite Brisk

Yesterday's sugar market production area telegram reported that the price of Cuban spot sugar rose by 0.03125, and the price of New York sugar futures rose by 0.02 for September, December, and May of next year. However, the price for March rose by 0.04. There was no change in the price of Java spot futures sugar. The Guild's registered 24th grade coarse-grained white sugar for Dutch sugar saw sluggish buying. Bids opened at $11.6 taels, but there were few inquiries. The transaction volume of medium-grained white sugar at $11 taels was also sparse, with the market being flat and weak. The transaction price for Taikoo Auto Sugar registered B mark was $12.1 taels, CW mark was $11.95 taels, DY mark was $11.8 taels, HX mark was $11.75 taels, and HM mark was $11.3 taels to $11.35 taels, showing an upward trend. The number of registered sales was very sparse. Jardine Matheson opened sales of 200 tons of 20th grade medium-grained white sugar for August shipment at a price of 5.5 Dutch guilders, with traders showing little buying interest, and was unable to sell them all at once.

Hardware: Black Iron Sheet Arrives Again, 500 to 600 Dan

Five to six hundred dan of black iron sheet arrived again yesterday, so the market price was slightly cheaper. 3' x 6' sheets were sold for $9.5 taels and 2' x 6' sheets were sold for $11.5 taels. Transactions were sluggish due to 客帮 discontinuing their purchases.

Factory Nails Drop in Price Due to Promotion of Sales

Hardware transactions have been very quiet recently, so the entire market sees scattered transactions. However, the price of factory nails was dropped by $0.02 due to the boycott of Eastern goods, in order to promote sales. It is estimated that each barrel costs $7.2 taels, as well as $7 taels. It is expected that there will definitely be hope for future trading development.

Local News

Today the Entire City Mourns for the Overseas Chinese

▲Anti-Japanese Association Committee Members Sworn In

The Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Committee, after its first committee meeting, resolved to mourn for the overseas Chinese victims in Korea this morning and to hold a ceremony for all committee members to take their oaths of office. The committee's current affairs meeting appointed eleven organizing committee members to form a preparatory committee to carry out the preparations. It is heard that all preparatory procedures have been completed as of yesterday. Today, all industrial and commercial circles in the city will close for half a day in the morning to express their condolences. All exchanges will also suspend trading in the morning. The banks have been notified by the Banking Association to all members to comply. The money industry has also decided by its association not to list in the morning. The New World Company has decided to close for half a day today. The Silk Factories Association yesterday notified all silk factories in Shanghai to suspend work for one day today. The Sixth District Public Bus Industry Union has issued an order to all members to suspend business for half a day today. As for the mourning ceremony, it will be held at 9:00 AM this morning in the City Chamber of Commerce. After the mourning ceremony, all committee members will take their oaths of office.

The Shanghai Special District Citizens' Federation held an emergency meeting of the entire preparatory committee for the anti-Japanese aid overseas Chinese matter at 8:00 PM the day before yesterday. More than twenty people attended. Chairman Zhang Yi gave a speech. The meeting began with a ceremony. (A) Reporting on incoming documents and the purpose of the meeting. (B) Discussing proposals. (1) Attending the memorial service and taking the oath at 9:00 AM on the 23rd. (2) Flying the flag at half-mast and closing for half a day on that day. (3) Distributing slogans and ensuring they are posted. (4) Urgently issuing a public announcement to the people to oppose Japan, printing and distributing it throughout the city. The above four points were ordered to be handled by the branch associations. (5) Soliciting plans from all circles. Received documents from Sang Maosheng, Hua Clan Association Zheng Nan, Jiading Ling family, Qiu Kedong, Lu Ziping, Bai Qiangsheng, Gao Fengxiang, Ji Xinpu, and others.

These will be transferred to the Anti-Japanese Association for review and reference.

The First Branch of the Shanghai Special District Citizens' Federation held a continued temporary executive committee meeting yesterday for the anti-Japanese aid overseas Chinese incident. Chairman Wang Lianfang, in addition to discussing and deciding on various practical measures for firmly severing economic ties with Japan, immediately notified all members, stating that: "Greetings, it has been decided by the temporary executive committee of this association, based on the measures set by the Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Committee and the notice from the general association of the Citizens' Federation, that all members of this association must fly the flag at half-mast on July 23rd and close for half a day in the morning to show their sincerity in mourning the overseas Chinese who died in Korea and to demonstrate the unity of the citizens' patriotic movement. Furthermore, the staff of each member's shop should voluntarily express their condolences in the shop and should not go out in order to maintain order. Please read, check, and implement. Enclosed is a printed copy for your reference and posting."

The Shanghai Antique Dealers Association, for the anti-Japanese aid overseas Chinese case, was convened by the chairman of the committee, Wang Hanliang, at 10:00 AM the day before yesterday, gathering industry members at the antique market to hold an anti-Japanese meeting. The meeting began with a ceremony. First, the chairman reported, then a notice was issued: (1) Close in the morning of the 23rd and fly the flag at half-mast for the entire day. (2) Post slogans. (3) Go to the swearing-in ceremony and mourn the overseas Chinese victims on the morning of that day. (4) Decide on six measures for economic severance. (Omitted for brevity)

Between 7:00 and 8:00 PM last night, some people were distributing anti-Japanese aid overseas Chinese leaflets in various roads in the Public Concession. They were arrested by the patrolling police and taken to the police station along with the leaflets. Those in the central district were detained in the Central Police Station on Fuzhou Road, totaling four people. Those on Sichuan Road and other places were detained in the Hongkou Police Station, totaling eight people.

Traffic and Public Utility Workers Will Not Stop Work This Morning

▲City Party Headquarters Notifies Various Labor Unions

The industrial and commercial sectors of the city will suspend business this morning to express their condolences, which has been requested by the Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Committee to the City Party Headquarters to notify various labor unions. However, whether workers in transportation and public utilities should stop work like other workers is not clearly stipulated by the Citizens Training Association. A certain labor union in the city had requested instructions from the Citizens Training Association on this matter. Recently, the Citizens Training Association replied to the labor union, stating that the nature of transportation and public utilities is different from other industries. As a rule, other industries stop work on memorial days, but these industries are always an exception. In order to maintain traffic in the city, they must not stop work this morning. The Citizens Training Association has informed the labor unions of the transportation and public utility industries of this intention.

Anti-Japanese Association to Begin Registering Japanese Goods Starting Today

▲A Large Batch of Japanese Goods Yesterday

▲Will Be Detained After Verification

The Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Committee, after telegraphing various places to detain Japanese goods, has begun inspection work in this city. Yesterday, more than 140 tons of Japanese goods were seized at the South Station of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway. The committee held its second plenary committee meeting yesterday and decided on many important cases. The details are as follows:

▲Detaining Japanese Goods The Anti-Japanese Association received a tip-off yesterday afternoon that a large batch of Japanese goods, more than 140 tons, including cotton yarn, eastern sugar, and seafood, was at the South Station of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway. The inspection department of the association sent personnel to investigate and confirmed the information. The association sent a letter to the Railway Bureau and the South Station, requesting that the goods be detained immediately and not allowed to be shipped out of Shanghai. The goods have now been seized and are awaiting disposal.

▲Start Registration The Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Committee of Shanghai announced the fifth order, starting the registration of Japanese goods. Since the resolution of the general assembly to permanently sever economic ties with Japan, the first committee meeting of the association decided on four measures for the disposal of Japanese goods and published them in the newspaper for various industries to comply with. It is now decided to start registering Japanese goods on July 23rd. All industries and shops must immediately register all existing Japanese goods with the registration department of the association. Do not delay, as it is of utmost importance.

▲Committee Meeting The association held its second plenary committee meeting at 5:00 PM yesterday, attended by Tao Baichuan, Wang Xiao _, Wang Yansong, Hou Dachun, Chen Tingrui, Chen Yafu, Zhang Huijun, Hu Fengxiang, Li Wenjie, Li Cishan, Liu Shimu, Zhang Yichen, Wang Xiaoying, Lin Kecong, Chen Songyuan, Wang Jian, Xi Yushu, Yan Esheng, Wang Wenhua, Chen Peide, Zhou Xuexiang, Zheng Chengqing, Feng Yixian, Lu Xingzhuang, Tang Junsheng, and other twenty-five people. Tao Baichuan was elected chairman. After the ceremony, the chairman reported on the resolutions of the standing committee meeting and the progress of various tasks. Then, Chen Songyuan reported on the design committee meeting, Wang Yansong reported on the economic committee meeting, and Zheng Chengqing reported on the preparations of the preparatory committee for mourning the overseas Chinese victims and various contacts. Next, the committee discussed various cases. (1) Discussing the nomination of deputy directors of various departments proposed by the standing committee for ratification. The deputy directors of each department are concurrently held by committee members. Previously, it was decided by the first committee meeting that, due to the urgency of the work, the first standing committee meeting decided to appoint Zheng Chengqing as deputy director of the general affairs department, Chen Yafu as deputy director of the propaganda department, Chen Peide as deputy director of the inspection department, Wang Wenhua as deputy director of the investigation department, Xi Yushu as deputy director of the registration department, and Zhang Yichen as deputy director of the storage department. The association sent letters to invite them to join the work, pending ratification at the next plenary committee meeting. A special request was made for ratification, which was approved. (2) Discussing the resignation of the standing committee member Lu Jingshi from all positions. It was resolved to retain him. (3) Discussing the registration method. It was resolved that: (A) Japanese goods imported before July 14th will be allowed to be registered by the association and then sold. The specific measures will be formulated separately, designating Chen Songyuan, Wang Jian, and Xi Yushu to draft them. (B) The registration period will be from the 23rd for a period of fifteen days. (C) A corresponding fee will be charged for the goods registered with the association. (D) Before the registration is completed, Japanese goods will not be allowed to be declared or sold. (4) Discussing the oath of office, which was approved. (5) Cases not discussed today will be continued at 1:00 PM tomorrow.

▲Inspections in Various Places Travelers from Anqing, Wuhu, and other places in Shanghai received telegrams from their respective regions yesterday, stating that after the seizure of Japanese goods, preparations have been made to strictly inspect Japanese goods at the wharves starting today. Once discovered, the disposal will be quite strict, so please stop handling goods to avoid being detained upon arrival. Therefore, they dared not try again.

▲Cotton Cloth Imports Suspended The Shanghai Cotton Cloth Trade Association held a temporary emergency meeting of members at 2:00 PM yesterday to discuss measures for severing economic ties with Japan. Chairman Chen Songyuan unanimously advocated and resolved to suspend the import of Japanese goods from today and implement economic severance with Japan. A special committee against Japan was also organized, and Yu Wenyuan, Shi Jiumao, Li Shiru, Li Yinbiao, Zhang Maorong, Lu Zhongtao, Wang Shangzhong, Bu Boxun, Lvqiu Peiqing, Yang Fuxin, Zhu Jiasheng, and alternate Yin Weichen and Wang Zijuan were appointed as standing committee members to discuss fundamental solutions.

▲Customs Declaration Refusal The Shanghai Customs Brokers Union held an emergency meeting at 4:00 PM yesterday to discuss ways to boycott Japanese goods. It was resolved to immediately notify all members to clear procedures and prepare to refuse Japanese goods. In addition, the Customs Brokers Union, in order to voluntarily refuse to load Japanese goods, is said to have scheduled a members' meeting on the 25th to discuss the measures.

▲City Federation Letter The City Federation issued an emergency notice to members regarding the anti-Japanese aid overseas Chinese matter, stating: "Regarding the emergency notice, Japan's bullying of China has been a constant occurrence since the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895. Recent examples include the forced Twenty-One Demands on May 9th, the massacre of Chinese citizens on May 30th, and the massacre of Jinan soldiers and civilians and diplomatic officials on May 3rd. Now, they have instigated the Korean people to massacre thousands of overseas Chinese, causing tens of millions in property damage. Such barbarity is resented by both gods and men and is intolerable to heaven and earth. How can we endure this? How can we remain silent in the face of this crisis of survival? In the past incidents of May 9th, May 30th, and May 3rd, we all resisted Japanese goods, bravely advanced, united as a nation, endured hardship, and shared the same hatred. The sacrifices were not small, but the results were like bubbles, and some even took the opportunity to advance their careers and get rich, losing their minds. As a result, we were ridiculed by the Japanese, who said that our enthusiasm was only five minutes. Hearing this mockery, our hearts are cut like knives. We cannot but be ashamed of the past. Now we are again engaging in economic severance with Japan. This term has been used many times. If we do not act with strength, how can we avoid the shame of the past? Members of our association, living under the iron heels of imperialists, have suffered hardships and have a clearer understanding. We must all resolutely and thoroughly resist Japanese goods and not be tempted by temporary profits, lest we bring shame upon ourselves and our country. This is a special emergency notice. We hope that all will swear to thoroughly resist Japan in order to uphold our nation and save our country. We deeply pray for this. The Shanghai Special District Citizens' Federation."

City Land Bureau Proclamation

▲Land Tax Collection Begins on August 1st

The City Land Bureau issued a proclamation yesterday, stating: "Regarding the proclamation, in accordance with the land tax (Mang Yin) for the 20th year in this city, collection is now scheduled to begin on August 1st. The tax rate for this year's land tax is 1.5 yuan of silver for the regular tax per tael, 0.25 yuan of silver for the city surcharge, 0.3 yuan of silver for the local surcharge, and 0.123 yuan of silver for the handling fee, totaling 2.173 yuan of silver. In addition, various surcharges, collectively known as 'levied jointly,' and municipal expenses will continue to be collected per mu as before and will be listed separately in the grain string (liangchuan). From the date of collection, there will be a limit of two months to pay in full, with the deadline being September 30th. Those who have not paid in full by the deadline will be charged an additional one-twentieth. The deadline will be extended for another two months, up to November 30th. Those who have not paid in full by the deadline will be charged an additional one-tenth as a penalty for late payment. In addition to reporting to the municipal government and issuing separate letters, this proclamation is hereby issued to all citizens of the city for their information. It must be known that paying taxes is the duty of the people. All businesses should pay the land tax and various jointly levied amounts in full within the time limit, prepare the string (liangchuan) and settle the business, and not delay. This order is of utmost importance."

Various Circles in the Three Districts Send Telegrams to Comfort Anti-Bandit Soldiers

▲Anti-Bandit Propaganda Conference Resolved Yesterday

Yesterday (the 22nd) at 10:00 AM, the Party Headquarters of the Three Districts of this city convened various circles to hold an anti-bandit propaganda conference in the auditorium of the Party Headquarters of the Three Districts in the Temple of the Queen of Heaven. Representatives from the Dyeing Industry Union of the Three Districts, the Shaoxing Seven Counties Association, the First Elementary School, the Public School of the Party Headquarters of the Three Districts, the Shuji Elementary School, Jiangnan College, the Wool Carding Trade Association, the Duck Slaughtering Operation Union, the Sand and Stone Industry Association, the Coal and Stone Barge Transportation Union, the Water and Electricity Industry Union of the Six Districts, the Education Association of the Three Districts, the Candy and Canned Food Industry Association, the Letterpress Printing Industry Association, and various branches, totaling about 300 people, were present. Sun Mingqi presided over the meeting. After the chairman reported on the significance of the meeting, Zhu Yingpeng, Tao Baichuan, and others gave speeches. Subsequently, a representative temporarily moved to send telegrams to comfort the anti-bandit soldiers, which was unanimously passed. The meeting then adjourned. The gist of the speeches is summarized as follows:

▲Summary of Speeches Zhu Yingpeng's speech briefly stated that there was originally no Communist Party in China ten years ago. After the reorganization of the Chinese Kuomintang in the Republic of China in 1924, the Communist Party took the opportunity to invade and steal party power. During this period, Russia established the Soviet government. Russia, which claims to be a revolutionary country of the proletariat, is actually a red imperialist. Many small countries that were previously annexed by Russia appear to be independent from the Russian Empire on the surface, but in fact they are still subordinate to it and have no political power. We can see the conspiracy of its means by looking at the Russian constitution. (1) The army cannot be organized by itself and must be organized by the Soviet government. (2) The financial budget cannot be decided by itself and must be decided by the Soviet Federation. (3) Diplomacy cannot be handled independently and must be decided by the Soviet Federation government. The ambition of this situation is obvious. The Chinese Communist Party is a running dog of Russia. How dangerous it would be if it were to steal political power. This time, the National Government is suppressing the rampant Red bandits in Hunan, Jiangxi, and other places, who are killing, setting fires, raping, and looting everywhere. This is truly work to save the people and the country. We want peace in China and a prosperous life for the people, so the Red bandits must be exterminated. I hope that the comrades and compatriots who are present today will take on the responsibility of oral propaganda and tell everyone about the disasters and dangers of these Red bandits. Following that, Tao Baichuan, a member of the executive committee of the City Party Headquarters, gave a speech, briefly stating that Mr. Zhu had already explained the significance of suppressing bandits and all the circumstances of Soviet Russia very clearly. The Communist Party often says outside that if China unites with Soviet Russia, it can receive equal treatment. Mr. Zhu just used the inequality of the Soviet Russian constitution as proof. I believe that there is now a very important key, that is, whether China will be annexed by Soviet Russia or whether it will work hard to exist on its own. We know that Japan invades China with the power of the Japanese, while Russia not only invades China with the power of the Russians, but also uses the Chinese themselves to invade China. This is the most terrible thing, because they use the general farmers and workers on one hand, and on the other hand, in Outer Mongolia and Southern Manchuria in our country, they allow young people to join the Communist Party, gather rogues, and organize the Red Army (Red bandits) to make trouble everywhere in our country, so that Chinese society cannot be peaceful and the people cannot live in peace. At the same time, they send troops to Manchuria and Mongolia to carry out aggression. This method of internal and external attacks is much more dangerous than Japan. Therefore, to save the country and save the people, we must support the National Government's suppression of the Red bandits. Now, the places with the most Red bandits are Jiangxi, Hunan, and other provinces. In the past year, more than 300,000 people in Hubei and Jiangxi provinces were killed by the Red bandits, more than 2 million were displaced and unable to return home, and more than 3 million houses were burned down. Jiangxi is the place with the most rice production, and more than 50 million dan of rice were burned by the Red bandits. The property lost due to the Red bandits in the two provinces is 100 million. If they are ravaged by the Red bandits for another two years, the future of China will be very dangerous. We must save the country by first suppressing the Red bandits. On the one hand, because of suppressing the Red bandits, we will not be afraid of being annexed by Soviet Russia. On the other hand, we can save the lives of the people. We are all patriotic and should rise up and unite to promote the truth. Younger children can give speeches to their fathers and brothers about the crimes of the Red bandits, so that the Red bandits will be eliminated in a matter of days. After Tao's speech, representatives Fan Gengxin and others gave successive speeches, the length of which is omitted for brevity.

▲Conference Telegram After the speeches were completed, Yu Zeren and Fan Gengxin, representatives of the Shaoxing Seven Counties Association in Shanghai, temporarily proposed that a telegram be sent in the name of the conference to comfort the generals at the front who are suppressing the bandits, which was unanimously passed.

Sino-Chilean Commercial Treaty to Be Handled in China

▲Embassy to Be Established in Beijing, Temporary Office to Be Set Up in Shanghai

▲Many Overseas Chinese in Chile, Relations with That Country Are Still Harmonious

▲Our Authorities Currently Intend to Conduct Sino-Chilean Shipping Route

The newly appointed Chilean Chargé d'Affaires to China, Mr. Bascuñán, recently arrived in Shanghai with his wife upon the orders of his government. After paying respects to our Minister of Foreign Affairs in Beijing, he has now returned to Shanghai from Beijing. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency interviewed him at the Waldorf Astoria Hotel on the Bund yesterday. His remarks are recorded as follows:

▲New Sino-Chilean Treaty It has now been decided to handle the new Sino-Chilean treaty in China. I came to China this time specifically for this matter. The contents of the treaty are divided into commerce and friendship. It was previously handled by the Chinese Chargé d'Affaires to Chile, Mr. Zhang, in Santiago, but had not reached the signing stage. After that, I will continue to handle it with the Chinese Ministry of Foreign Affairs.

▲Establishing an Embassy The Chilean government intends to select a suitable location in Nanjing to build a new embassy. I have already made contact with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs during my visit to Beijing this time. However, due to the selection of the location and the construction time, it cannot be realized in a short time. Therefore, for this transition period, it is planned to set up a temporary agency in Shanghai to facilitate communication with the outside world at any time. However, I still need to telegraph the government for instructions before making a decision.

▲Overseas Chinese in Chile Although I don't know exactly how many overseas Chinese are in Chile, there are quite a few. Most of them are mainly engaged in business or industrial enterprises and are very wealthy. They are all amiable and approachable, so the people of China and Chile have very harmonious and close relations. Mr. Zhang was also very welcomed by all sectors of our country in Chile. During my visit to Beijing this time, Minister Wang also told me that he plans to establish a Sino-Chilean shipping route to make the commerce between the two countries more developed. In this way, I firmly believe that the relations between China and Chile will be even closer.

▲Impressions of China Before I came to China, I had long heard that China is an ancient country with a highly civilized and long history. After arriving in China, I realized that this statement is still not false. In addition to admiring China's civilization and the development of all industries, I am also very grateful for the kind hospitality of the Chinese government, Minister Wang, and all sectors of society.

▲Also a Reporter Mr. Bascuñán finally said that he was also a journalist more than ten years ago and felt quite interested in the journalistic career. After leaving the journalistic career, he entered the diplomatic field and has been in it for thirteen or fourteen years. He served as a Chilean diplomat in Poland for several years.

Customs Brokers Request the Suppression of Foreign Merchants

▲Because No Country Allows Foreigners to Establish Customs Brokerages

▲To Prevent Japanese Merchants from Speculating During Patriotic Movements

The customs brokers in this city are concerned about the trend of foreign merchants gradually monopolizing the customs brokerage industry in our country. Whenever Chinese merchants engage in patriotic movements and boycott Japanese goods, foreign merchant customs brokerages often seize this opportunity to undertake loading and shipping, so it is actually no different from not stopping loading. This only causes intangible losses to Chinese merchants. Moreover, no country allows the establishment of foreign merchant customs brokerages. In the past, the government strictly suppressed foreign merchants from paying taxes on behalf of customers. However, this is not the case in the tax country. There are more than 800 Chinese merchant customs brokerages in this city, including Yuanfeng, China Merchants Yu, etc. There are more than 30 Japanese merchant customs brokerages, including Higuchi, Yamaguchi, and Masuki. There are four British merchant customs brokerages, including Hengmao and Maotai. Japanese merchants account for three-tenths of the total business in the city. Before the May 9th National Humiliation Day occurred, there were only one or two foreign merchant customs brokerages in China, which only declared and loaded goods for foreigners. Since May 9th, when the Chinese people rose up to boycott Japanese goods, Chinese merchant customs brokerages unanimously refused to load them. Japanese merchants took the opportunity to set up their own customs brokerages. At that time, the Jianghai Customs did not prohibit it, resulting in great losses for Chinese merchants. When May 3rd and May 30th occurred, Chinese merchant customs brokerages also refused to load Japanese goods, and the result was still the same. To this day, the influence of Japanese customs brokerages is already deep. The goods of merchants from Dalian, Niuzhuang, and other places are now taken away by Japanese merchant customs brokerages. Japanese merchant customs brokerages intend to lower prices. For example, for one piece of cotton yarn, the Chinese merchant customs brokerage price is 2.3 taels, while the Japanese merchant price is 1.6 taels. If this continues, without quickly devising fundamental countermeasures, Chinese merchant customs brokerage will decline due to patriotic movements. Therefore, in addition to planning to send representatives to the Jianghai Customs Supervisory Office to petition within the next few days, the industry has also prepared a petition to the City Party Headquarters and the City Chamber of Commerce, requesting that they forward a letter to the Jianghai Customs to suppress foreign merchant customs brokerages in order to maintain commerce and protect national rights.
